GRE阅读机经470篇分篇幅专项练习，短文章每篇一般160词左右，推荐控制在4分钟内做完。实际考试的时候，Section1 会有1篇短文章，Section2自适应会有2篇短文章。

 

Passage 2 Medium

As it was published in 1935, Mules and Men, Zora Neale Hurston's landmark collection of folktales, may not have been the book that its author first had in mind. In this anthropological study, Hurston describes in detail the people who tell the stories, often even inserting herself into the storytelling scene. Evidently, however, Hurston had prepared another version, a manuscript that was recently discovered and published after having been forgotten since 1929. This version differs from Mules and Men in that it simply records stories, with no descriptive or interpretive information.

While we cannot know for certain why Hurston's original manuscript went unpublished during her lifetime, it may have been because publishers wanted something more than a transcription of tales. Contemporary novelist and critic John Edgar Wideman has described Black literature as the history of a writing that sought to escape its frame, in other words, as the effort of Black writers to present the stories of Black people without having to have a mediating voice to explain the stories to a non-Black audience. In this, Hurston may have been ahead of her time.

landmark陆标，地标；里程碑，转折点；<美>有历史意义的建筑（或遗址）

folktales民间故事；民间传说

anthropological人类学的；人类学上的

interpretive解释的；作为说明的

transcription抄写，打印；抄本，文字记录

Black literature黑人文学：主要是指美国黑人作家创作的文学作品，这些作品通常反映了黑人在美国的生活经历、文化传统和社会问题。

mediating调停

佐拉-尼尔-赫斯顿（Zora Neale Hurston）具有里程碑意义的民间故事集《骡子和人》出版于 1935 年，这可能不是作者最初设想的那本书。在这本人类学研究著作中，赫斯顿详细描述了讲故事的人，甚至经常把自己融入讲故事的场景中。不过，赫斯顿显然还准备了另一个版本，这份手稿自 1929 年被遗忘后，最近才被发现并出版。这个版本与《骡子和人》的不同之处在于，它只是记录故事，没有任何描述性或解释性信息。

虽然我们无法确定赫斯顿的原稿为何在她生前没有出版，但这可能是因为出版商想要的不仅仅是故事的记录。当代小说家和评论家约翰-埃德加-维德曼（John Edgar Wideman）将黑人文学描述为一部试图摆脱框架的写作史，换句话说，黑人作家努力展现黑人的故事，而不必通过中介的声音向非黑人读者解释这些故事。在这一点上，赫斯顿可能走在了时代的前列。

Passage 6 Easy

Although some skeptics points to Arctic places such as the high latitudes of Greenland, where temperatures seem to have fallen, a recent scientific report concludes that in recent decades average temperatures have increased faster in the Arctic than elsewhere. Scientists have long suspected that several factors lead to greater temperature swings at Earths polar regions than elsewhere. First, most of the Arctic is covered in snow and ice, which are highly reflective; if snow and ice melt, the exposed soil, which absorbs heat, serves to accelerate warming. Second, the polar atmosphere is thin, so little energy is required to warm it. Third, less solar energy is lost in evaporation at the frigid poles than in the tropics.

skeptics疑论者，怀疑主义者（skeptic 的复数形式）

latitude [地理]纬度，某一纬度地区

swing摆动，摇荡 v&n

frigid寒冷的，严寒的；冷淡的

尽管一些持怀疑态度的人指出，格陵兰岛等北极高纬度地区的气温似乎有所下降，但最近的一份科学报告得出结论说，近几十年来，北极地区的平均气温比其他地区上升得更快。科学家们长期以来一直怀疑，有几个因素导致地球极地地区的气温波动比其他地区更大。首先，北极大部分地区被冰雪覆盖，冰雪具有很强的反射性；如果冰雪融化，裸露的土壤会吸收热量，从而加速气候变暖。其次，极地大气稀薄，因此只需要很少的能量就能使其变暖。第三，与热带地区相比，寒冷的极地因蒸发而损失的太阳能更少。

In pointing to the apparent temperature change in the high latitudes of Greenland, the skeptics mentioned in the passage intend to raise as a question whether

A Greenland is less likely to experience extreme temperature changes than are other areas of the Arctic.

B Those more localized temperature drops might indicate an important trend not captured by the upward trend of average Arctic temperatures.

C There might be a reversal of the temperature trend in the high latitudes of Greenland.

D The factors that cause temperature change in the high latitudes of Greenland are different from those that affect the rest of the Arctic.

E Greenland has more ice and snow on the ground than do other areas of the Arctic.

文中提到的怀疑论者在指出格陵兰岛高纬度地区明显的温度变化时，打算提出一个问题

与北极其他地区相比，格陵兰岛不太可能经历极端的温度变化。

那些更局部的温度下降可能表明了一个重要的趋势，没有被北极平均温度的上升趋势所捕捉到。

在格陵兰岛的高纬度地区，温度趋势可能会发生逆转。

导致格陵兰岛高纬度地区温度变化的因素与影响北极其他地区的因素不同。

格陵兰岛上的冰雪比北极的其他地区都要多。

reversal反转，颠倒；（运气）逆转；挫折，失败；（角色的）交换，互换

答案：B

该题干【文中skeptics提到格棱兰地区温度变化时，想要提出一个问题】，也就是问skeptics提到格棱兰地区温度下降的目的。定位到首句，可知他们认为格棱兰地区的温度是下降的，跟整个北极地区温度上升的趋势不一致，也就是B选项“这些局部的温度下降可能表明了一个重要的趋势，没有被北极整体平均的气温上升趋势体现出来。”。

C选项表述不当，意为“格陵兰高纬度地区的温度趋势可能会发生逆转”，原文并没有说要“逆转” ，skeptics只是说这个格陵兰高纬度地区的趋势可能和整个北极地区的趋势不同。

Passage 9 Medium

An Irish newspaper editorial encouraging women to participate in the non-importation movement launched in Ireland in 1779 appears consistent with a perception that the political use of the consumer boycott originated in North America and spread eastwards across the Atlantic to Ireland. This is a view that most historians have concurred with. For example, T.H. Breen argued that the consumer boycott was a brilliantly original American invention. Breen did acknowledge that a few isolated boycotts may have taken place in other countries. However, Mary O'Dowd argues that from the late seventeenth century, Irish political discourse advocated for the nonconsumption of imported goods and support for home manufactures by women in ways that were strikingly similar to those used later in North America.

editorial

  • adj.编辑的，主编的；社论的

  • n.社论，社评；（报刊的）由编辑撰写的部分，非广告部分

non-importation禁止进口；不进口

perception看法，认识；感觉，感知；洞察力

concur同意，赞同；（事件）同时发生

discourse演讲，论述；谈话，交流

一份爱尔兰报纸的社论鼓励妇女参加 1779 年在爱尔兰发起的不进口运动，这似乎与消费者抵制的政治用途起源于北美并横跨大西洋向东传播到爱尔兰的观点一致。大多数历史学家都同意这一观点。例如，T.H. 布林（T.H. Breen）认为，消费者抵制是美国的一项杰出的原创发明。布林承认，其他国家可能也发生过一些孤立的抵制活动。不过，玛丽-奥多德（Mary O'Dowd）认为，从 17 世纪晚期开始，爱尔兰的政治言论就倡导妇女不消费进口商品并支持家庭制造，其方式与后来在北美使用的方式惊人地相似。

In the context of the passage, the highlighted sentence serves to

A qualify a point made in the preceding sentence

B correct an erroneous assumption

C provide evidence in support of a perception cited in the opening sentence为开头句中的观点提供证据

D provide a rationale for the view expressed in the following sentence

E establish the popularity of a point of view

Qualify有熟词生义“If you qualify a statement, you make it less strong or less general by adding a detail or explanation to it.”

rationale <正式>根本原因，逻辑依据

答案：B。高亮的句子为“Breen did acknowledge that a few isolated boycotts may have taken place in other countries."这一句的上一句是说 Breen 认为抵制消费活动起源于美国.而高亮句是 Breen 做的让步（通过acknowledge这个词可以得出），说明他也承认有一些例外的情况。那对应到A选项，在限制他自己在上一句提出的观点。

Passage 11 Hard

Before feminist literary criticism emerged in the 1970s, the nineteenth-century United States writer Fanny Fern was regarded by most critics (when considered at all) as a prototype of weepy sentimentalism--a pious, insipid icon of conventional American culture. Feminist reclamations of Fern, by contrast, emphasize her "non-sentimental" qualities, particularly her sharply humorous social criticism. Most feminist scholars find it difficult to reconcile Fern's sardonic social critiques with her effusive celebrations of many conventional values. Attempting to resolve this contradiction, Harris concludes that Fern employed "flowery rhetoric" strategically to disguise her subversive goals beneath apparent conventionality. However, Tompkins proposes an alternative view of sentimentality itself, suggesting that sentimental writing could serve radical, rather than only conservative, ends by swaying readers emotionally, moving them to embrace social change.

prototype原型，雏形；典型，范例；蓝本，最初形态

weepy眼泪汪汪的；要哭的；催人泪下的

sentimentalism感伤主义，感情主义；多愁善感

pious虔诚的；敬神的；可嘉的；尽责的

insipid无味的，清淡的；无趣的，无活力的

reclamation开垦；收回；再利用；矫正

reconcile调和，使协调一致；（使）和解，（使）恢复友好关系；调停

sardonic讽刺的；嘲笑的，冷笑的

effusive流露感激之情的；（火山岩）喷发的；（岩浆）大量喷发的

rhetoric花言巧语，浮夸之词；修辞，修辞学

disguise假扮，伪装；掩饰，隐瞒

sentimentality多愁善感

在20世纪70年代女权主义文学批评出现之前，19世纪的美国作家范妮·芬(Fanny Fern)被大多数评论家(如果被考虑的话)视为哭泣感伤主义的原型——一个虔诚、平淡的传统美国文化的象征。相比之下，女权主义者对弗恩的评价则强调她“不多愁善感”的品质，尤其是她犀利幽默的社会批判。大多数女权主义学者发现，很难将弗恩对社会的讽刺批评与她对许多传统价值观的热情洋溢的庆祝结合起来。为了解决这一矛盾，哈里斯得出结论，弗恩策略性地使用“华丽的辞藻”来掩饰她在明显的传统之下的颠覆性目标。然而，汤普金斯提出了多愁善感本身的另一种观点，他认为多愁善感的写作可以服务于激进的，而不仅仅是保守的，通过在情感上动摇读者，促使他们接受社会变革。

The passage suggests which of the following about the "contradiction" mentioned in the highlighted sentence?

A It was not generally addressed by critics before the 1970s.

B It is apparent in only a small number of Fern's writings.

C It has troubled many feminist critics who study Fern.

address <正式>（向某人）提出（陈述、投诉等）。另一方面可以理解contradiction不是一个可以被解决的问题？

【答案】AC 【题型】推断题 【解析】该题问这对高亮句中矛盾的正确表述。A 在1970s之前这个矛盾没有被普遍提出。我们结合原文第一句和第二句，在1970s之前女权主义没有出现，critics只认识到了sentimental这个特点。注意这个矛盾由两个矛盾面组成(sentimental和social critiques)，而另一面也就是social critiques是feminists出现之后他们认识到的。所以也就是feminists出现之前这个矛盾肯定是没有被普遍提出的，所以A对。C选项可从第3句Most feminist scholars find得知。B选项无中生有。

It can be inferred from the passage that Tompkins would be most likely to agree which of the following about the "critics" mentioned in the passage?

A They accurately characterize the overall result Fern is aiming to achieve.

B They are not as dismissive of Fern as some feminist critics have suggested.

C They exaggerate the extent to which Fern intended her writing to serve a social purpose.

D They wrongly assume that "sentimental" must be a pejorative term.

E They fail to recognize the role that sentimental rhetoric plays to readers' emotions.

从文章中可以推断，汤普金斯最有可能同意以下哪一项关于文章中提到的“批评家”?

它们准确地描述了芬想要达到的总体结果。

他们并不像一些女权主义评论家所说的那样轻视弗恩。

他们夸大了弗恩写作的社会目的。

他们错误地认为“多愁善感”一定是一个贬义词。

他们没有认识到感伤修辞对读者情感的作用。

characterize描述，刻画；成为……的特征，是……的典型

dismissive轻蔑的，鄙视的，不加考虑的，不屑一顾的

pejorative轻蔑的，贬损的；恶化的，变坏的

【答案】D 【题型】推断题 【解析】该题问T最会支持的针对文章中评论者的表述。T的观点立场体现在最后一句：T提出针对感情主义自身的替代解释：可以通过左右读者情感方式服务激进变革目标。DE选项之中，D选项更好。之前评论者有insipid的明显负评。原文末句T的观点，等于承认之前评论者至少认识到感情主义可以服务于保守主义目标，不能等同于E选项（完全意识不到情感主义的作用）。

A T认为 critics正确表达了Fern想要实现的目标。critics并没有表达出来这个目标，是T表达出来了。

B T认为critics没有女权评论家认为的对于Fern不屑一顾。文章里面没有这个对比，也没有dismissive这个态度。

C T认为critics夸大了Fern想要让她的写作去服务于一个社会目的的程度。critics没有表达出来社会目的，是T表达出来了，所以C错。

 

Passage 13 Easy

Biologists have long debated about whether egg production in birds is biologically highly costly, some theorizing that egg production is energetically or nutritionally demanding. Lack, however, suggested that clutch size-the number of eggs a bird lays per breeding cycle-is far below the potential limit of egg production. He suggested that clutch size had instead evolved in relation to the number of young that the parents could successfully rear. Subsequently, most studies focused on limitations operating during chick rearing, particularly among altricial species (species in which the parents feed their young in the nest). Lack later recognized that in precocial species (species in which young feed themselves), clutch size might be explained by different factors-the availability of food for egg-laying females, for example.

rear养育，饲养；栽种，培植；（动物）用后腿直立；（建筑、山等）高耸

 

Passage 14 Medium

Carla L. Peterson`s Doers of the Word (1997), a study of African American women speakers and writers from 1830-1880, is an important addition to scholarship on nineteenth-century African American women. Its scope resembles that of Frances Smith Fosters 1993 study, but its approach is quite different. For Foster, the Black women who came to literary voice in nineteenth-century America were claiming their rights as United States citizens, denying that anything should disqualify them from full membership in an enlightened national polity. Peterson sees these same women as having been fundamentally estranged from the nation by a dominant culture unsympathetic to Black women, and by a Black intelligentsia whose male view of race concerns left little room for Black female intellect.

scholarship奖学金；学问，学术

scope范围，领域；（发挥能力的）机会，施展余地；视野，眼界

deny否认；拒绝承认；拒绝给予

disqualify取消……的资格

estrange使疏远；离间

intelligentsia知识分子；知识界

concerns担心；关心的事，关注点

Carla L. Peterson 的 Doers of the Word（1997 年）是对 1830-1880 年间非裔美国女演说家和女作家的研究，是对 19 世纪非裔美国妇女学术研究的重要补充。其研究范围与 Frances Smith Fosters 1993 年的研究相似，但研究方法却截然不同。在福斯特看来，19 世纪美国黑人妇女在文学上发出自己的声音，是在主张自己作为美国公民的权利，她们不承认任何事情会剥夺她们作为开明国家政体正式成员的资格。彼得森则认为，这些黑人女性从根本上与国家疏远，因为主流文化对黑人女性缺乏同情心，黑人知识分子对种族问题的男性观点也没有给黑人女性的智慧留下多少空间。

The passage indicates that Peterson identifies which of the following as obstacles faced by the women included in her study?

A the attitudes of Black male intellectuals toward female intellectual work

B the discriminatory attitudes faced by Black women in nineteenth-century America as a whole十九世纪美国黑人妇女整体面临的歧视态度

C disagreements among Black women speakers and writers themselves about the impact of the Black intelligentsia

intellectuals [劳经]知识分子（intellectual 的复数）

答案：AC

It can be inferred that Peterson`s study and Fosters study are similar with respect to which of the following?

A the writers that each takes up for examination

B the degree to which each has influenced other scholars

C the assumptions that each brings to nineteenth-century African American literature

D their analysis of the nineteenth-century Black intelligentsia

E their interpretation of nineteenth-century Americas dominant culture

【答案】A 【题型】推断题 【解析】此题问的是Peterson和Fosters研究的相似之处，定位到原文的“Its scope resembles that of Frances Smith Fosters 1993 study, but its approach is quite different." 一句，可知答案是【its scope】，但具体是什么范围呢？ 注意【遇到指示代词，往前看】，看上一句，会发现Carla L. Peterson’s Doers of the Word (1997), a study of African American women speakers and writers from 1830-1880，所以p的研究范围时一些非裔美国女作家和演说家。因此范围相同，就是p和f两个人都研究同一批对象。所以根据这个，直接选到A the writers (that each takes up for examination), 意思是：每个学者（each）分析研究的writers，是一样的。 至于其他选项，degree程度，interpretation解读/看法，analysis分析，assumption假设/看法，都不是我们要的scope，排除。

Passage 15 Medium

David Belasco`s 1912 Broadway production of The Governors Lady created a sensation with a scene set in a Childs cafeteria, a chain restaurant that was an innovator in food standardization and emblematic of modern everyday life. While Belasco`s meticulously detailed reproduction of an immediately recognizable setting impressed the public, it was derided by progressive theater critics who championed the New Stagecraft theories of European artists like Max Reinhardt. The New Stagecraft rejected theatrical literalism; it drew inspiration from the subjectivity and minimalism of modern painters, advocating simplified sets designed to express a dramatic texts central ideas. Such critics considered Belasco a craftsman who merely captured surface realities: a true artist eliminated the inessential to create more meaningful, expressive stage images.

Broadway百老汇（美国纽约市戏院集中的一条大街）

sensation感觉，知觉；感觉能力，知觉能力；轰动，引起轰动的人（或事）

emblematic象征的；可当标志的

deride嘲笑，愚弄，揶揄

progressive

  • adj.进步的，先进的；逐步发生的，逐步发展的；向前移动的；（音乐）现代的，新潮的；（税制，税种）累进的；（动词）进行式的；（纸牌游戏，舞蹈）搭档轮换的

  • n.进步分子，改革派人士；进行时（或体）

champion捍卫，拥护，支持

literalism拘泥于字句；直译主义；彻底写实主义

大卫·贝拉斯科(David Belasco) 1912年在百老汇创作的《总督夫人》(The Governors Lady)引起了轰动，其中一个场景发生在儿童自助餐厅，这家连锁餐厅是食品标准化的创新者，也是现代日常生活的象征。虽然贝拉斯科一丝不苟地重现了一个一眼就能认出来的场景，给公众留下了深刻的印象，但却遭到了进步的戏剧评论家的嘲笑，他们支持马克斯·莱因哈特(Max Reinhardt)等欧洲艺术家的新舞台艺术理论。新舞台艺术拒绝戏剧直译主义;它从现代画家的主观性和极简主义中汲取灵感，提倡简化的场景设计，以表达一种戏剧性的文本中心思想。这些评论家认为贝拉斯科是一个只捕捉表面现实的工匠:一个真正的艺术家会消除不必要的东西，创造出更有意义、更有表现力的舞台形象。

The author of the passage implies which of the following about Belasco`s production of The Governors Lady? 关于贝拉斯科的作品《总督夫人》，作者暗示下列哪项?

A It was dismissed by certain theater critics who misunderstood Belasco`s conception of modernity. 某些戏剧评论家误解了贝拉斯科对现代性的概念，因此对这部剧不屑一顾。

B It was intended to marshal elements of the New Stagecraft to serve Belasco`s predilection for realistic staging. 它的目的是将新舞台艺术的元素整合起来，以满足贝拉斯科对现实主义舞台的偏好。

C It demonstrated that theatrical literalism could be used effectively to express a dramatic texts central ideas. 这表明戏剧直译主义可以有效地表达戏剧文本的中心思想。

D It elicited responses that reflected a discrepancy between popular tastes in entertainment and the tastes of progressive theater critics. 它所引起的反应反映了流行的娱乐品味和进步的戏剧评论家的品味之间的差异。

E It relied on the appeal of an impressively realistic stage set to compensate for weaknesses in other aspects of the production. 它依靠令人印象深刻的逼真舞台布景的吸引力来弥补制作中其他方面的不足。

marshal整理（思路、想法等）

discrepancy差异，不符

答案：D

It can be inferred that the theater critics would be most likely to agree with which of the following statements about the theatrical productions?

A Theatrical productions that seek to eliminate the inessential also often eliminate theatrical elements that enhance the expressiveness of a play. 试图剔除不必要内容的戏剧作品往往也会剔除增强戏剧表现力的戏剧元素

Passage 17 Easy

Early naturalists believed two species of beaver lived in North America: dam beavers and bank beavers. The bank species was thought to resemble the muskrat in behavior, living in burrows or lodges and unable to build dams. In fact, dams are primarily a strategy for dealing with annual variations in water levels. If water levels fall in summer, as they do in most of North America, then beavers lodge entrances may be exposed. With stabilized water levels, their homes are much safer. Along deep rivers, where bank beavers are found, this problem seldom arises. But these beavers do know how to build dams, and do so if the need arises, as may occur if they are forced to relocate after felling and consuming all nearby trees.

lodge

  • v.（使）固定，（使）卡住；（通常付住宿费地）借住，寄住，（为某人）提供住宿；存放，寄放（贵重物品）；正式提出（投诉、要求等）；铭记，留存

早期的博物学家认为北美生活着两种海狸:坝狸和岸狸。河岸物种被认为在行为上与麝鼠相似，生活在洞穴或小屋中，无法建造水坝。事实上，大坝主要是一种应对每年水位变化的策略。如果夏季水位下降，就像北美大部分地区一样，海狸的住所入口可能会暴露出来。水位稳定了，他们的家就安全多了。在河狸出没的深河里，这个问题很少出现。但这些海狸确实知道如何建造水坝，如果有需要，它们就会这样做，因为在砍伐和消耗了附近所有的树木后，它们可能被迫搬迁。

 

The passage provides support for which of the following statements about beaver dams?

A One important function of these dams is to protect beavers homes.

B Most are built prior to burrow construction.

Passage 28 Easy

Early life insurers in the United States found themselves facing the problem of obtaining reliable information, as they needed to rely on applicants themselves to provide truthful, complete answers to a standard set of questions. In an attempt to personalize the relationship between insurers and their individual applicants, firms selected highly respected local citizens to act as their agents. These agents were expected to evaluate the appearance of candidates, unearth evidence of unhealthy family histories or questionable habits, and attest to the respectability of the people writing testimonial letters on an applicant's behalf. In short, the initial purpose of the agency system was not to actively solicit customers, but, rather, to recreate the glass-bowl mentality associated with small towns or city neighborhoods.

Passage 29 Easy

For years, the leading theory for what caused the Younger Dryas (a dramatic reversal, about 12,900 years ago, in a global warming trend) was a release of water from Glacial Lake Agassiz. The theory posited that this meltwater flooded into the North Atlantic, lowering the salinity and intensity of surface waters enough to prevent them from sinking. Ocean currents were changed in such a way that northward transport of heat in the ocean diminished, and the North Atlantic regions plunged back into near-glacial conditions. However, evidence has emerged that the Younger Dryas began long before freshwater flooded the North Atlantic. Additionally, the temperature changes induced by a shutdown in the North Atlantic heat conveyor system are too small to explain the Younger Dryas.

reversal反转，颠倒；（运气）逆转；挫折，失败；（角色的）交换，互换；<法律>（对下级法院或权力机构裁决、宣判或法令的）撤销，废弃；

posit<正式>假设，认定；建立在（假说）上（posit sth. on）；安置，放置

salinity盐度；盐分；盐性

intensity强烈，剧烈；（光、声音等的）强度

plunge back重新投入：重新开始或投入某项活动或工作。

induced by引起

conveyor传送带，传送装置；传播者，传达者

多年来，关于造成 “少干期”（约 12900 年前全球变暖趋势的急剧逆转）的主要理论是阿加西兹冰川湖融水的释放。该理论认为，这些融水涌入北大西洋，降低了表层海水的盐度和强度，足以阻止它们下沉。洋流发生了变化，海洋中向北输送的热量减少，北大西洋地区重新陷入近冰川时期的状态。然而，有证据表明，早在淡水涌入北大西洋之前，幼年干旱期就已经开始了。此外，北大西洋热量输送系统关闭引起的温度变化太小，不足以解释少干纪。

Passage 30 Easy

One reason researchers have long believed that Mars never enjoyed an extensive period of warm and wet climate is that much of the surface not covered by wind-borne dust appear to be composed of unweathered material. If water flowed for an extended period, researchers reasoned, it should have altered and weathered the volcanic minerals, creating clays or other oxidized, hydrated phases (minerals that incorporate water molecules in their crystal structure) .

It turns out, though, that the scientists were not looking closely enough. New high-resolution mapping data and close-up surface studies have revealed clays and other hydrated minerals in many regions. The clay deposits are scattered all over, in ancient volcanic surfaces and heavily cratered highland regions, some of which have apparently been exposed by erosion only recently.

长期以来，研究人员一直认为火星从未经历过长时间的温暖潮湿气候，原因之一是火星表面未被风尘覆盖的大部分区域似乎由未风化的物质组成。研究人员推断，如果水长期流动，就会改变和风化火山矿物，形成粘土或其他氧化的水合相（晶体结构中含有水分子的矿物）。

但事实证明，科学家们观察得不够仔细。新的高分辨率绘图数据和表面特写研究揭示了许多地区的粘土和其他水合矿物。这些粘土沉积物散布在古老的火山表面和火山口密集的高原地区，其中一些显然是最近才被侵蚀暴露出来的。

Passage 31 Easy

Scientific consensus is that humans first began to have a warming effect on Earth`s climate within the past century, after coal-burning factories, power plants, and motor vehicles began releasing carbon dioxide (CO2) and other greenhouse gases in significant quantities into the air. However, evidence suggests that human agricultural activities may have had such an effect much earlier: concentrations of CO2 started rising about 8000 years ago, even though natural trends indicate they should have been dropping; methane levels rose similarly about 3,000 years later. Without these rises, however, current temperatures in northern parts of North America and Europe would be cooler by three to four degrees Celsius-enough to inhibit agriculture-and an ice age would probably have begun several thousand years ago in northeastern Canada.

consensus一致看法，共识

methane甲烷，沼气

Celsius（温度）摄氏的

inhibit抑制，约束；使拘束，使尴尬；降低（酶等）的活性

科学界一致认为，人类最早开始对地球气候产生变暖影响是在上个世纪，即烧煤的工厂、发电厂和机动车开始向空气中大量释放二氧化碳（CO2）和其他温室气体之后。然而，有证据表明，人类的农业活动可能在更早的时候就已经产生了这样的影响：二氧化碳的浓度在大约 8000 年前就开始上升，尽管自然趋势表明它们应该在下降；甲烷的浓度在大约 3000 年后也出现了类似的上升。然而，如果没有这些上升，北美和欧洲北部地区目前的气温将降低三到四摄氏度--足以阻碍农业的发展--冰河时期可能早在几千年前就在加拿大东北部开始了。

Passage 34 Easy

Archaeologists studying Bonito phase (ca. A.D. 900-1140) Native American ceramics from Chaco Canyon, New Mexico, observed that many pots had been altered after firing to revise their decorative designs--usually, intricate geometric patterns painted in black on white slipped surfaces. In some cases, a new design was imposed over an earlier one; less often, the original design was simply covered with white slip. Crown and Wills doubt that the alterations were made to correct design errors. Many Chaco pots with design errors were left unaltered. Furthermore, when errors were corrected, revisions were made prior to firing-either by painting directly over the error or by scraping off designs and applying new slip and paint, which is a less time-consuming method than repainting and refiring flawed pots.

ceramics制瓷艺术，陶艺；陶器，陶瓷制品

Chaco Canyon查科峡谷，位于美国新墨西哥州西北的纳瓦约印第安人保留地。如今，这里气候干燥，草木不生。

geometric几何图形的；几何的，几何学的

impose强制推行，强制实行；把（自己的观点、信仰等）强加于；打扰，麻烦；

prior to在……之前，先于

scrape off刮掉：通过刮的动作去除某物。

文章翻译：两个非作者观点，第二个反对第一个考古学家在研究来自新墨西哥州查科峡谷的波尼托期(约公元900-1140年)美国原住民陶器时发现，许多陶器在烧制后都被修改过，以修改其装饰设计--通常是在白色滑面上用黑色画出复杂的几何图案。在某些情况下，新的设计被强加在先前的设计之上;较少的情况是，原来的设计被简单地用白色滑液覆盖。Crown和wi11s怀疑这些改动并不是为了纠正设计错误。许多有设计错误的查科壶都没有被修改。此外，当错误被纠正时，修改是在烧制前进行的--要么是直接在错误处上色，要么是刮掉设计并涂上新的滑石和涂料，这比重新上色和完善有缺陷的壶要省时。

Because the subject matter was so personal, the work of several prominent mid-twentieth century poets has been termed "confessional" poetry. But confession is a bad metaphor for what those poets did. The motive for confession is penitential or therapeutic-by speaking openly about personal guilt and suffering, the poet hopes to make them easier to bear. But these poets always approached their writing as artists, and their motive was aesthetic. Writing from experiences like madness, despair, and lust, their aim was to make effective art, not to cure themselves. To treat their poems mainly as documents of personal experience is not just to diminish the poets` achievement, but to ignore their unanimous disdain for the idea of confessional poetry.

prominent重要的，著名的；显眼的，突出的；突起的，高耸的

metaphor隐喻，暗喻；象征，标志

penitential

  • adj.赎罪的；后悔的；悔罪的

  • n.悔罪规则书；悔罪者

therapeutic

  • adj.治疗的，有疗效的；使人镇静的，使人放松的；治疗学的

  • n.疗法，治疗药物；治疗学（therapeutics）

lust

  • n.性欲；强烈欲望；（神学，被看作是罪过的）感官欲望

  • v.有强烈的性欲；渴望

unanimous（投票、决定、协议等）全体同意的，无异议的；（所有人）一致同意的，意见一致的

disdain

  • n.鄙视，蔑视

  • v.鄙视，蔑视；不屑（做某事）

诗人没有做什么?

A.认为写作动机和对诗歌评判是有关的(文中没提到这些诗人是否要用motive，对motive的讨论都是本文作者的讨论)

B.通过写诗缓解个人的痛苦遭遇(错误不以这个为目的不意味着没有受到缓解)

Astronomers who study planet formation once believed that comets-because they remain mostly in the distant Oort cloud, where temperatures are close to absolute zero-must be pristine relics of the material that formed the outer planets. The conceptual shift away from seeing comets as pristine relics began in the 1970s, when laboratory simulations revealed there was sufficient ultraviolet radiation reaching comets to darken their surfaces and there were sufficient cosmic rays to alter chemical bonds or even molecular structure near the surface. Nevertheless, astronomers still believed that when a comet approached the Sun-where they could study it-the Sun`s intense heat would remove the corrupted surface layer, exposing the interior. About the same time, though, scientists realized comets might contain decaying radioactive isotopes that could have warmed cometary interiors to temperatures that caused the interiors to evolve.

comet彗星

pristine整洁的，崭新的；未受损害的，处于原始状态的；正派的，正直的

relic遗迹；遗骸；纪念物

laboratory simulations实验室模拟

ultraviolet

  • adj.紫外的，紫外线的；（设备，技术）产生紫外线的

  • n.紫外光，紫外辐射

isotope同位素

decaying radioactive isotopes衰变的放射性同位素

研究行星形成的天文学家曾经认为，彗星——因为它们大部分停留在遥远的奥尔特云中，那里的温度接近绝对零度——一定是形成外层行星的物质的原始遗迹。从20世纪70年代开始，将彗星视为原始遗迹的观念开始转变，当时实验室模拟显示，到达彗星的紫外线辐射足以使彗星表面变暗，而宇宙射线也足以改变彗星表面附近的化学键甚至分子结构。尽管如此，天文学家仍然相信，当一颗彗星接近太阳时——他们可以对其进行研究——太阳的强烈热量会除去损坏的表层，暴露出内部。然而，大约在同一时间，科学家们意识到彗星可能含有衰变的放射性同位素，这些同位素可能会将彗星内部加热到导致内部进化的温度。

【文章结构分析】 文章开头介绍老观点：彗星曾经被认为是纯粹的形成外部行星的残留物。 然后说1970年开始的新认识：紫外线放射足以使其表面不纯。Nevertheless转折后，说，太阳的热度足以剥除彗星表面的不纯物质，意思是彗星仍然可以是纯粹的。文章最后说，彗星本身的放射性同位素足以使其内部演化，意思是彗星更可能是不纯的。

According to the passage, astronomers recognize which of the following as being liable to cause changes to comets?

A cosmic rays

B radioactive decay

C ultraviolet radiation

【答案】ABC 【题型】事实信息题 【解析】该题需要选项定位。定位到原文“laboratory simulations revealed there was sufficient ultraviolet radiation reaching comets to darken their surfaces and there were Sufficient cosmic rays to alter chemical bonds or even molecular structure near the surface”可知选AC选项，根据原文comets might contain decaying radioactive isotopes that could have warmed cometary interiors to temperatures that caused the interiors to evolve可知B选项。

According to the passage, astronomers` belief that comets are pristine relics was

A overturned by analysis of what happens when comets approach the Sun被“分析彗星接近太阳所发生的情况”所推翻(是被1970s的实验推翻的)

B supported by what observations revealed about the composition of the outer planets被“揭示带外行星成分的观察”所支持最后一句暗示了这一点是被质疑的内容)

Carolina Hospital notes that Cuban-American writers who write primarily in English are dismissed from anthologies and analyses of Cuban exile literature on that account. She argues that since these writers were born in Cuba and consider themselves Cuban writers, they should not be ignored, and maintains that they represent a new phase of Cubanness, one that is expressed in the language comfortable to its writers-English. Moreover, another critic notes that the Spanish and English traditions of Cuban-American writing have different but equally viable functions. The English branch seeks to create a distinctive culture of Cuban roots in the United States, whereas the Spanish branch wishes to preserve a specifically Cuban culture while seeking affiliation with the canon of Latin American letters.

anthologies [图情] 选集

exile

  • n.流放；被流放者，流亡者

  • v.流放；使离开

affiliation（与政治、宗教等组织的）联系，从属关系；加盟，加入

canon <正式>准则，标准；教规，宗教法规；作品集，精品集；经典；真经，正经；卡农（一种复调音乐）；大教堂教士，（主教座堂的）咏礼司铎；（罗马天主教）律修会修士；（作为罗马天主教弥撒一部分的）祭献经文

卡罗莱纳指出，主要以英语写作的古巴裔美国作家因此被排除在古巴流亡文学的选集和分析之外。她认为，由于这些作家出生在古巴，自认为是古巴作家，他们不应被忽视，并坚持认为他们代表了古巴的新阶段，这是用作家所熟悉的语言-英语来表达的。此外，另一位评论家指出，古巴裔美国人的西班牙语和英语写作传统不同，但同样可行。英语分会力求在美国创造一种独特的古巴根源文化，而西班牙分会则希望保留一种特别的古巴文化，同时寻求与拉丁美洲字母的经典联系。

所有古巴裔美国作家都被公认为对古巴流亡文学有贡献。

In the context in which it appears, "comfortable" most nearly means

A prosperous 繁荣的，富足的

B sufficient 足够的，充足的；（理由、条件）充足的，充分的

C agreeable （适合的，令人愉悦的）愉悦的，讨人喜欢的；欣然同意的；可接受的

D restful 宁静的；安静的；给人休息的

E painless 无痛的；不痛的

正确答案：C

 

painless作为“不费劲的”的英文释义：involving little effort or stress. agreeable的英文释义为：enjoyable and pleasurable。 个人觉得其实两个都可以，但是agreeable可能更好（虽然我当时秒选了painless QAQ）如果换成painless感觉更多是在强调这些作者对英语“也可以使用”，没有突出CH想强调的这些作者对英语”非常熟练“所以才使用英语写小说。 有点类似于，小明的母语是中文，而英文也学得不错，所以他写小说首选的语言是中文。这时我会形容他的中文”agreeable“，用的特别熟练，可以轻松地拿来写小说；而他的英文使用起来是“painless”，可以正常交流但不至于说“agreeable”

Exotic insect pests can produce both short-and long-term effects on forest ecosystems. Short-term effects include the disturbances directly associated with the action of the pest, which may cause the defoliation, loss of vigor, or death of trees. Long-term effects are primarily mediated by changes in tree species composition and the consequent alterations of forest structure, productivity, and nutrient uptake. Exotic pests are more efficient than most abiotic disturbances (e.g., fire or wind) at producing long-term changes in species composition. Pests often target specific tree species and, if they become established, they usually remain as permanent components of the ecosystem. Shifts in forest species composition ramify through the ecosystem in many ways because tree species have different, often unique properties.

exotic

  • adj.奇异的，异国风情的

  • n.外来植物，外来动物

pest 害虫，有害动物；<非正式>讨厌的人（或物）

disturbance干扰，扰乱；骚乱，动乱；失调，紊乱

defoliation落叶，去叶；[植] 脱叶

vigor [生物]活力，精力

mediate

  • v.调停，斡旋；影响……的发生，使……可能发生；促成（协议），找到……的解决办法；引起，形成；传递，传达；连接，沟通；处于中间地位

  • adj.间接的；居间的，介于中间的

composition成分构成，成分；（音乐、艺术、诗歌的）作品；创作，作曲；构图；作文

abiotic非生物的，无生命的

ramify（使）分枝，分叉；成网状

The passage mentions which of the following as effects of exotic pests on forest ecosystems?

A decreased vitality in trees

B defoliation of trees

C changes in forest structure

答案：ABC

vitality 活力，热情；生机，生命力

The author of the passage mentions the "unique properties" of tree species primarily in order to help explain

A why pests tend to target specific tree species

B why pests can have long-term effects on entire ecosystems（long-term其实没法看出来）

C how pests contribute to shifts in forest species composition

D how pests are able to become established in an ecosystem

E how some tree species are able to withstand the effects of pests

【答案】C 【题型】细节目的题 【解析】定位到原文“Shifts in forest species composition ramify through the ecosystem in many ways because tree species have different, often unique properties”可知unique property可以解释的就是为什么shifts in forest ramify through（森林树种组成不断变化），因此选C。

A：该信息不是解释为什么pests target different species，而是说明 pests target different species 的结果是什么。正是由于不同pest的target不同，而不同的树种有不同特性所以一旦外来pest在某个森林中settle down之后，会影响森林的composition。

B：这个信息的位置在尾句 相关联的直接信息就是forest species shift ；unique property 是[为森林树种改变的结果不同]来提供理由的 ，而不是为long-term 提供理由的 根据文章逻辑 实际上 long term effect本身指由于受到树种改变影响而出现的森林结构、产量和营养摄入的变化（Long-term effects are primarily mediated by changes in tree species composition and the consequent alterations of forest structure, productivity, and nutrient uptake.）所以这里的逻辑应该是两条线：

①不同树种有unique property 导致 由于昆虫带来的森林树种结构变化不一样（ Shifts in forest species composition ramify through the ecosystem in many ways because tree species have different, often unique properties）

②森林树种结构变化 会影响到森林的structure、productivity and nutrient intake使其改变 而这三方面的改变才是long term effect

两条逻辑线整理清楚后 就能清楚看到 unique property其实和long term没有直接的因果关系 它只是用来说明森林树种改变的原因罢了

D 解释pest establish的过程，与原文不符

E 原文未提及这个内容。

For centuries, oak was the wood of choice for European shipbuilders. However, toward the end of the eighteenth century, as British oak supplies grew scarce, shipbuilders there turned to teak and found in it an ideal substitute. Other woods expand and contract at different rates than oak, so repairs to oak ships done with those woods split or leak. Only teak matches oak`s expansion coefficient and stays watertight. It is unmatched in its resistance to rot and pests, and its oils even protect nails against corrosion. Moreover, it was one of two important tropical hardwoods (with Central American mahogany) that dried light enough to float downriver--the only way to transport timber in quantity from the inland jungles where it grew.

oak橡树，栎树；橡木，栎木

teak柚木

contract

  • n.合同，契约；<非正式>暗杀协议；（桥牌）定约墩数；婚约，订婚

  • v.（使）收缩，缩小；签合同，订立契约；患上，感染；订立婚约（或盟约）；欠负（债）

coefficient（数）系数；（物理）率，系数

watertight（容器或房间）防漏水的，水密的；（理论、计划或协议）严密的，无懈可击的

unmatched无与伦比的；不相配的；无匹敌的

rot

  • v.（使）腐败，（使）腐烂；逐渐衰弱（或憔悴）；<英，旧，非正式>取笑，开玩笑

  • n.腐烂，腐烂物；<英>腐化，堕落（the rot）；<美>官员腐败（the rot）；（尤指植物的）枯病

nail钉子；指甲

in quantity在某物的数量或数量方面，可以表示某物的数量增加或大量生产某物

From the 1880s to the 1930s, the textile industry in Japan employed over half of all workers, most of them in the three major branches of silk reeling, cotton spinning, and weaving. Because the branches were highly diverse-in scale, skill requirements, and technology-historians traditionally have analyzed them separately. However, the workforces of all three were drawn primarily from the same population: young, mostly rural women aged 10 to 25. Noting this commonality, Hunter argues that a consideration of the three branches of production together is long overdue: examining elements common to the different branches of textile production may, she asserts, permit the identification of gender-based factors that may have influenced the operation of the Japanese female labor market as a whole.

When studying shrimp feeding from hydro-thermal vents at the bottom of the ocean, biologists were surprised that the shrimps` reproductive cycles followed seasonal patterns. Far beyond the reach of sunlight, and with food abundant around the vents all year round, why should such animals reproduce seasonally? The answer might involve their offspring, which in their larval form drift in the currents to colonize new vents. The larvae must feed during their trip, and their springtime release coincides with a peak in algae raining down from surface waters. So far, researchers have found no evidence of seasonal breeding among vent-dwelling species that provide their offspring with yolk to sustain them or among vent-dwelling species found in areas of the ocean with not seasonal algae blooms.

shrimp虾，小虾

hydro-thermal热液的；热水的

vent火山口

reproductive生殖的，繁殖的；翻印的，复制的

offspring（人的）后代，子女；（动物的）幼崽，崽兽；结果，产物

larval幼虫的；幼虫状态的；潜在的；隐蔽的

larvae幼虫，幼体（larva 的复数）

springtime春天；春季；初期

algae水藻，海藻

dwelling

  • n.住宅，住所，公寓

  • v.居住（dwell 的现在分词形式）

yolk蛋黄；[胚] 卵黄；羊毛脂

在研究从海底热液喷口取食的虾时，生物学家惊讶地发现虾的繁殖周期遵循季节性模式。在远离阳光的地方，在通风口周围全年都有丰富的食物，为什么这些动物要季节性繁殖呢?答案可能与它们的后代有关，它们以幼虫的形式在洋流中漂流，在新的喷口定居。幼虫必须在旅途中进食，它们的春季释放正好与从地表水中落下的藻类高峰相吻合。到目前为止，研究人员还没有发现任何证据表明，在为后代提供卵黄以维持生命的喷口物种中，或者在没有季节性藻类繁殖的海洋地区发现的喷口物种中，有季节性繁殖的迹象。

【文章结构分析】

文章是典型的现象解释结构。首先引入特殊现象：生物学家发现居住在海底、不依赖太阳光源的虾的繁殖有季节性规律。可能性解释：和它们的后代繁殖有关，因为后代迁移的时候需要食物，而作为食物的海藻的供给量是有季节性的。换句话说虾的季节性繁殖的原因是吃春天的海藻。

Which of the following best describes the function of the highlighted sentence?

A It casts doubt on the accuracy of earlier observations of seasonal breeding among shrimp species living near hydro-thermal vents. 这使人们对生活在热液喷口附近的虾类季节性繁殖的早期观察结果的准确性产生了怀疑。

B It undermines the explanation proposed for seasonal breeding among some shrimp species living near hydro-thermal vents. 它破坏了对生活在热液喷口附近的一些虾类季节性繁殖的解释。

C It suggests that alternative theories are needed to explain seasonal breeding among shrimp species living near hydro-thermal vents. 这表明需要其他理论来解释生活在热液喷口附近的虾类的季节性繁殖。

D It describes the survival benefits to shrimp of mating in parts of the ocean where algae blooms rain down abundantly. 它描述了在藻类大量繁殖的海洋地区交配对虾的生存好处。

E It supports the explanation proffered for the seasonal breeding observed among some shrimp species living near hydro-thermal vents. 它支持了对生活在热液喷口附近的一些虾类所观察到的季节性繁殖的解释。

【答案】E

【题型】高亮句子功能题

【解析】本题问高亮句作用。从文章结构分析可知，高亮句应该为作者的观点提供支持：研究者发现为后代提供食物的物种并没有季节性繁殖的现象，并且居住在有非季节性开花的海藻的区域的物种也没有季节性繁殖的特征。也就是说如果海藻有季节性，繁殖也有季节性，海藻没季节性，繁殖也没季节性，因此是从反面论证了前文结论的正确性。选E。这个题要弄清楚一种论证方式：反证法。反证法的论证过程如下：首先提出论题：然后设定反论题，并依据推理规则进行推演，证明反论题的虚假；既然反论题为假，原论题便是真的。虾的季节性繁殖是因为吃春天的海藻，最后一句话说在没有海藻的地方是没有季节性繁殖的证据；不吃海藻（吃yolk）的物种也没有季节性繁殖的证据，反面不成立也就支持了正面的观点。

A 高亮句质疑之前观察的准确性，错误，高亮句是支持前面的观点。

B 高亮句反驳了解释，错误，高亮句是支持了前面的观点。

C 高亮句表明需要另外的解释，错误，高亮句就是在支持前面的解释。

D 高亮句描述了虾的交配的好处，错误，和这个无关。

Which of the following statements about hydrothermal vents can be inferred from the passage?

A They can propel newly released shrimp larvae toward other vents that are nearby.

B Some of them are found in areas of the ocean with no seasonal algae blooms.

C The food they provide for species living near them does not become seasonally scarce.

【答案】BC 【题型】推断题 【解析】A.该选项成立条件有三：1.运动主体-larvae 符合文章/2.动力来源-vents（propel）文章无充足信息支撑这一点/3.运动路径-从一个vent到其附近的另一个vent 文章无信息支撑这一点。综上，文章信息只能得出larvae会离开其出生的vent但这种运动的起因以及具体轨迹，文章未讨论。因此A不选。

B.根据原文So far, researchers have found no evidence of seasonal breeding among vent-dwelling species that provide their offspring with yolk to sustain them or【 among vent-dwelling species found in areas of the ocean with not seasonal algae blooms】.可以得出B选项；（到目前为止，研究人员还没有发现任何证据表明，在为后代提供卵黄以维持生命的喷口物种中，或者在没有季节性藻类繁殖的海洋地区发现的喷口物种中，有季节性繁殖的迹象。）

C.根据原文Far beyond the reach of sunlight, and with food abundant around the vents all year round, 可知shrimps所在的vents全年食物丰富可以得出C选项

There have been numerous well-documented extinctions of indigenous species caused by the introduction of non-indigenous predators and pathogens. However, surprisingly few extinctions of indigenous species can be attributed to competition from introduced species. For example, during the past 400 years, 4,000 plant species have been introduced into North America, and these non-indigenous plants currently account for nearly 20 percent of North America`s plant species. Yet no evidence exists that any indigenous North American plant species became extinct as a result of competition from new species could mean that such extinctions take longer to occur than scientists initially believed or, alternatively, that extinctions are rarely caused by competition from non-indigenous species.

indigenous本土的，固有的

pathogen病原体，致病菌

由于引入非本地捕食者和病原体，已经有大量的本地物种灭绝记录。然而，令人惊讶的是，很少有本土物种的灭绝可以归因于来自引进物种的竞争。例如，在过去的400年里，有4000种植物被引入北美，这些非本土植物目前占北美植物物种的近20%。然而，没有证据表明任何北美本土植物物种是由于新物种的竞争而灭绝的，这可能意味着这种灭绝的发生时间比科学家最初认为的要长，或者，灭绝很少是由非本土物种的竞争引起的。

正确答案：E

The physicist Wallace Sabine pioneered the scientific study of architectural acoustics when he was asked in 1895 to fix a university lecture hall in which the echo of a speaker`s words rendered them unintelligible. He found that the length of time it takes a sound`s echo to decay is determined by the absorption of the sound`s original energy by surrounding material. By hanging panels of sound-absorbing felt on the walls, Sabine reduced the echo enough to make the hall usable. And the data he compiled yielded a mathematical formula for the relationship between a room`s echo duration, its quantity and quality of sound-absorbing materials, and its spatial volume.

architectural建筑学的，建筑方面的；与建筑物相似的；

acoustics声学；音响效果，音质

render使成为，使处于某种状态；给予，提供；（以某种方式）表达，表现

unintelligible莫名其妙的；无法了解的

absorption (液体、气体等的)吸收；吸纳，同化；专注，着迷；（液体、气体等的）吸收

panel

  • n.专家咨询组，专题讨论小组；（门等的）镶板，嵌板；控制板，仪表盘；（车身的）金属板；（衣服上的）镶条，饰片；画板；<美>陪审团；<英>国民保健制度（原国民健康保险）医师名单；<苏格兰，法律>被告

  • v.用（木板、金属板等）覆盖，镶

spatial空间的，与空间有关的；空间理解能力的

物理学家华莱士·萨宾(Wallace Sabine)开创了建筑声学的科学研究。1895年，他被要求修复一所大学的讲堂，因为讲者说话时发出的回声使人听不清。他发现，声音回声衰减所需的时间长短取决于周围物质对声音原始能量的吸收。通过在墙上悬挂吸音毡，Sabine减少了足够的回声，使大厅可用。他收集的数据产生了一个数学公式，用于计算房间的回声持续时间、吸声材料的数量和质量以及空间体积之间的关系。

The discovery of subsurface life on Earth, surviving independently from surface life, refuted the belief that biological processes require not only liquid water but sunlight as well, thus greatly enhancing the possibility of life beyond Earth. Take Jupiter's moon Europa. Space probes show a body covered with a thick layer of ice. As Europa orbits its planet, however, it flexes due to the gravitational tug-of-war between it, its sister moons, and Jupiter. Through friction, this flexing produces heat in the moon's interior capable of melting ice. Indeed, observations suggest liquid water exists beneath Europa's icy crust. Photosynthetic life is impossible there because sunlight is completely absent, but life such as the microbes that flourish deep within earth may still be possible.

地球上独立于地表生命存活的地下生命的发现，驳斥了生物过程不仅需要液态水，还需要阳光的观点，从而大大提高了地球以外存在生命的可能性。以木星的卫星木卫二为例。太空探测器显示了一具覆盖着厚厚的冰层的尸体。然而，当木卫二围绕它的行星运行时，由于它、它的姐妹卫星和木星之间的引力拉锯战，它会弯曲。通过摩擦，这种弯曲在月球内部产生了能够融化冰的热量。事实上，观测表明木卫二冰冷的地壳下存在液态水。因为那里完全没有阳光，所以没有光合作用的生命是不可能的，但是像微生物这样在地球深处繁衍生息的生命还是有可能存在的。

Soil communities are dependent on plants for organic matter. Plants provide organic matter for soil communities through the decomposition of leaf litter, by oozing nutrients from roots, or through other methods of deposition of organic compounds into the soil environments. As a result of these diverse methods by which plants supply resources, unique soil communities form under different plant species and under plant communities that differ in composition. If a nonnative plant species invades an above-ground community of flora and fauna, it can alter links between the native above-ground community and the below-ground soil community. For example, an invading nonnative plant could alter the quantity of leaf litter production, which would alter nutrient contributions to the soil.

Recent studies of the gender gap in the history of United States policies tend to focus on candidate choice rather than on registration and turnout. This shift in focus from gender inequality in political participation may be due to the finding in several studies of voting behavior in the United States that since 1980, differences in rates of registration and voting between men and women are not statistically significant after controlling for traditional predictors of participation. （人们可能不再那么关注政治参与中的性别不平等问题，这是因为在几个关于美国投票行为的研究中发现，自1980年以来，在控制了传统上影响政治参与的因素之后，男性和女性在注册投票和实际投票的比例上差异并不具有统计学意义。）However, Fullerton and Stern argue that researchers have overlooked the substantial gender gap in registration and voting in the South. While the gender gap in participation virtually disappeared outside the South by the 1950s, substantial gender differences persisted in the South throughout the 1950s and 1960s, only beginning to decline in 1970s.

最近对美国政策历史上性别差异的研究往往侧重于候选人选择，而不是登记和投票率。这种对政治参与中的性别不平等的关注转变可能是由于对美国投票行为的几项研究发现，自1980年以来，在控制了传统的参与预测因素后，男女之间的登记率和投票率的差异在统计上并不显著。然而，富勒顿和斯特恩认为，研究人员忽视了南方在登记和投票方面的巨大性别差距。到1950年代，南方以外地区在参与方面的性别差距几乎消失，但在整个1950年代和1960年代，南方仍然存在着巨大的性别差异，直到1970年代才开始缩小。

Recent studies of ancient Maya water management have found that the urban architecture of some cities was used to divert rainfall runoff into gravity-fed systems of interconnected reservoirs. In the central and southern May Lowlands, this kind of water control was necessary to support large populations throughout the year due to the scarcity of perennial surface water and the seasonal availability of rainfall. Some scholars argue that the concentration of water within the urban core of these sites provided a centralized source of political authority for Maya elites based largely on controlled water access. Such an argument is plausible; however, it is less useful for understanding the sociopolitical implications of water use and control in other, water-rich parts of the Maya region.

Ralph Ellison was passionately interested in visual arts. He immersed himself in Harlem`s art scene in the 1930s, even apprenticing with sculptor Richmond Barthe for a time. Our terrestrial food supply comes from ecosystems transformed to produce a few comestible species through the removal of competitors, predators, and pests, but marine capture fisheries depend on the overall productivity of natural ecosystems. There is, however, increasing concern about the impact of fishing and other human activities on marine ecosystems, which are now far from pristine. One option for moving toward both biodiversity and terrestrial food supply goals is to produce greater yields from less land, thereby freeing land for conservation purposes. By contrast, the objective of maintaining or resorting the biodiversity of marine ecosystems may conflict with the objective of maintaining or increasing our food supply from the sea, since the level of fishing required to achieve the latter may compromise the former.

  • n.食物

  • adj.可食用的

  • adj.海洋的，海产的；海运的，海事的

  • n.水兵，海军陆战队士兵；（一个国家的）船舶

pristine整洁的，崭新的；未受损害的，处于原始状态的；正派的，正直的

move toward朝……移动：向某个方向或目标移动。

Compromise

  • n.折中，妥协；妥协方案，折中办法

  • v.妥协，让步；危及，损害

我们的陆地食物供应来自于生态系统的转变，通过消除竞争对手、捕食者和害虫，产生一些可食用的物种，但海洋捕捞渔业依赖于自然生态系统的整体生产力。然而，人们越来越担心捕鱼和其他人类活动对海洋生态系统的影响，这些生态系统现在远非原始状态。实现生物多样性和陆地粮食供应目标的一个选择是用更少的土地生产更多的粮食，从而腾出土地用于保护目的。相比之下，维持或利用海洋生态系统生物多样性的目标可能与维持或增加海洋食物供应的目标相冲突，因为实现后者所需的捕捞水平可能会损害前者。

According to the passage, increasing the food yield per unit of land can have which of the following effects?

A enabling more land to be used for development purposes

B compromising progress toward conservation goals

C helping protect comestible species from competition and predation

D helping reduce pressure on marine ecosystems

E helping restore the biodiversity of terrestrial ecosystems

compromising progress toward conservation goals 请你帮我分析一下这个短语的语法构成 这个短语“compromising progress toward conservation goals”由几个部分组成： 1.主语（Subject）: 这个短语作为一个整体，可以被视作一个名词短语，其中的主语是“progress”。这里“progress”指的是向某个目标的进展或前进。 2.动词（Verb）: “compromising”是现在分词，在这里作为形容词使用，修饰“progress”。它传达了这样的信息：这个进展是以某种妥协为代价的，可能会影响其效果或质量。 3. 介词短语（Prepositional Phrase）: “toward conservation goals”是一个介词短语，用来进一步说明“progress”的方向或目标。其中，“toward”是介词，表示方向，“conservation goals”是介词的宾语，指的是保护和保存相关的目标。 将这些部分组合起来，整个短语描述的是一种可能会损害或削弱保护和保存目标的进展情况。这个短语可以被用在更大的句子中，例如：“The recent decision to open the protected area to tourism is compromising progress toward conservation goals.”（最近决定开放保护区给旅游业，这可能会损害保护和保存目标的进展。）

 

 

 

 

【答案】E

【题型】事实信息题

【解析】定位到原文produce greater yields from less land，thereby freeing land for conservation purposes，结合和海洋渔业的对比，可知E选项。

A 使更多土地用于发展目的。原文未提及

B 损害了环保目标的进展。和原文意思相反

C 帮助保护可食用物种免受竞争和捕食。原文未提及

D 帮助减少对海洋生态系统的压力。题目问的信息与陆地生态系统有关，和海洋无关

In various writings from the 1940s on popular culture, George Orwell examined commercial texts such as comics and crime novels, seeking out political meanings that ran counter to what he considered an inherent tendency toward socialism in the English common people. The public, he concluded, was often being duped by a convert patrician conservatism, conveyed through commercial culture, that restrained the people`s radical instincts. These works constituted some of Orwell` s greatest writing, yet those who see him as a lone precursor to today`s cultural studies, a field in which scholars examine the ideological implications of popular culture, are mistaken. A number of left-wing writers in the 1930s, many of them associated with the Communist Party, saw the need to take popular culture seriously.

在20世纪40年代关于流行文化的各种著作中，乔治·奥威尔研究了漫画和犯罪小说等商业文本，寻找与他认为英国普通人固有的社会主义倾向背道而驰的政治含义。他的结论是，公众经常被一种转变为贵族的保守主义所欺骗，这种保守主义通过商业文化传播，抑制了人们的激进本能。这些作品构成了奥威尔最伟大的作品之一，然而，那些认为他是当今文化研究(一个学者研究流行文化的意识形态含义的领域)的唯一先驱的人是错误的。20世纪30年代，许多左翼作家(其中许多人与共产党有联系)认为有必要认真对待流行文化。

The passage suggests which of the following about George Orwell?

A He regarded commercial texts a vehicles for the views of ordinary people. 选项无依据。在文章中，ordinary people是商业文本的作用对象。

B He regarded many commercial texts as having an insidious effect on readers.

【文章结构分析】 文章是研究介绍加评论结构。George Orwell 研究商业文本，认为其抑制普通民众的本能社会主义倾向，公众的激进本能(社会主义倾向)会被商业文本中convert patrician conservatism所蒙蔽。作者George Orwell的这些研究高评价, 但认为有早于George Orwell的对流行商业文化的严肃研究。

In recent decades, scholars of American literature have skillfully revealed authors` simultaneous accommodation（适应） and resistance（抵制） to an increasingly commercialized, capitalized environment during the early nineteenth century. Historians of the period have not, however, fully exploited literary criticism, due to the disciplinary boundaries that mark contemporary academic research. Few historians have extensive training in critical theory and its specialized languages, and the sheer volume of work in early American history and literature challenges anyone who would master either field, much less both. Moreover, historians study people across the nation, but much literary scholarship called "American" actually examines works produced in northeastern states. And historians usually study the operations of capitalism in its details, while literary critics produce a generalized picture of literary commodification.

近几十年来，美国文学学者巧妙地揭示了19世纪初作家们对日益商业化、资本化的环境既适应又抵制。然而，由于当代学术研究的学科界限，这一时期的历史学家并没有充分利用文学批评。很少有历史学家在批判理论及其专门语言方面受过广泛的训练，而美国早期历史和文学方面的大量工作对任何一个领域都精通的人来说都是挑战，更不用说两者都精通了。此外，历史学家研究全国各地的人，但许多被称为“美国人”的文学奖学金实际上研究的是东北部各州的作品。历史学家通常研究资本主义运作的细节，而文学评论家则描绘出文学商品化的总体图景。

A the amount of scholarship that they produce

B the nature of their geographic focus √

C the extent to which they are critical of early capitalism

D the extent to which they are interested in interdisciplinary study

E the extent to which they restrict their focus to a particular time period

C historian`s lack of interest in critical theory

D the distinctive nature of much literary criticism

E the ahistorical quality of much literary criticism

【答案】D

【题型】事实信息题

【解析】定位到原文对矛盾的解释：Few historians have extensive training in critical theory and its specialized languages, .... And historians usually study the operations of capitalism in its details, while literary critics produce a generalized picture of literary commodification. 可知文学批评的独特的性质是阻碍历史学家的研究的原因，所以选D选项。

A选项：overly thematic approach/过度主题化的处理方式，未提及

B选项： conservative notion 保守概念，未提及

C选项：lack of interest 未提及

E选项：ahistorical quality，意思是“很多文学评论的非历史性的特征”，注意，历史学家无法利用文学学者产物的原因，是因为缺乏专业的文学评论方法训练，以及历史学科和文学学科之间的天然差异/界限，而不是说，只要文学评论里有一些内容与历史无关，就无法研究了，因此ahistorical quality，文章未提及这一种因素

In 1755 British writer Samuel Johnson published an acerbic letter to Lord Chesterfield rebuking his patron for neglect and declining further support. Johnson`s rejection of his patron`s belated assistance has often been identified as a key moment in the history of publishing, marking the end of the culture of patronage. However, patronage had been in decline for 50 years, yet would survive, in attenuated form, for another 50. Indeed, Johnson was in 1762 awarded a pension by the Crown-a subtle form of sponsorship, tantamount to state patronage. The importance of Johnson`s letter is not so much historical as emotional; it would become a touchstone for all who repudiated patrons and for all who embraced the laws of the marketplace.

acerbic尖刻的（等于 acerb）；酸的；辛辣的

Lord

  • n.主，上帝；（英国）贵族，勋爵；大人，阁下（英国对某些官员的尊称）；（中世纪欧洲的）领主，庄园主；（英国）上议院议员；（某一领域的）巨头，巨擘

  • v.对某人举止霸道（或逞威风）；把……封为贵族

rebuke

  • v.<正式>斥责，指责

  • n.指责，叱责，训斥

patron（艺术家的）赞助人，资助者；代言人，名义赞助人；（酒吧、旅馆等的）主顾，顾客；（古罗马）有权势的保护人，庇护人

belated迟来的；误期的

patronage赞助，资助；（对餐馆、酒店或其他生意的）惠顾，光顾；职位授予权，恩惠给予权；庇护，扶植

attenuated

  • adj.（力量或效果）衰减的；（人）瘦长的

  • v.使减弱；使变细；稀释（attenuate 的过去式和过去分词）

pension

  • n.养老金，退休金；（法国和其他一些欧洲国家的）廉价小旅店；<史>（给皇室宠臣、艺术家或学者以便他们能从事公益工作的）津贴，补助金

  • v.（尤指因年龄或疾病而）向（某人）支付养老金使其退休；（因陈旧或不再有用而）丢弃（某物）

tantamount同等的；相当于……的

1755年，英国作家塞缪尔·约翰逊(Samuel Johnson)给切斯特菲尔德勋爵(Lord Chesterfield)写了一封尖刻的信，指责他的赞助人忽视了他，并拒绝进一步的支持。约翰逊拒绝了他的赞助人迟来的援助，这通常被认为是出版史上的一个关键时刻，标志着赞助人文化的终结。然而，50年来，赞助一直在减少，但在接下来的50年里，赞助将以弱化的形式存在。事实上，约翰逊在1762年获得了英国王室的养老金——这是一种微妙的赞助形式，相当于国家的赞助。约翰逊这封信的重要性与其说是历史上的，不如说是情感上的;它将成为所有拒绝庇护者和所有信奉市场法则的人的试金石。

The author of the passage mentions Johnson's 1762 pension award in order to

A reveal that Johnson remained consistent in his rebuke of Lord Chesterfield well after 1755在1755年之后，约翰逊对切斯特菲尔德勋爵的指责始终如一

B provide evidence for a general trend in the latter half of the eighteenth century of private patronage's being replaced by state sponsorship为18世纪下半叶私人赞助被国家赞助所取代的大趋势提供了证据

C situate the debate over the end of patronage within the wider realm of eighteenth-century economic history将关于赞助制度终结的争论置于18世纪经济史的更广阔领域中

D suggest that Johnson's letter to Chesterfield was noticed by the Crown only years after it was published约翰逊给切斯特菲尔德的信在发表几年后才被王室注意到

E emphasize that patronage still helped support Johnson's writing after his letter to Chesterfield强调在约翰逊给切斯特菲尔德的信之后，赞助人仍然支持着他的写作

【答案】E 【题型】细节目的题 【解析】注意原句开头的逻辑词“事实上”， 表明对前⽂的⼀种反转， 也就是表明约翰逊实际上仍然在接受资助， 并不是如开头的通⾏观点所表明的那样， 他的信标志着赞助⽂化的结束。

选项 A， 恰好相反，约翰逊⼜接受了赞助，所以不⼀致。A 错。

选项 B， 并不存在私⼈赞助被国家赞助替代的⼤趋势，看⽂章结尾，是赞助被市场⾏为代替。B错。

选项 C， 上⼀句可以认为是在讨论赞助的结束，但这⼀句说约翰逊在继续接受赞助，不能认为是在讨论赞助的结束。C错。

选项 D， 和“得到王室注意”没关系。D错。

选项 E， 符合作者观点，反对“信标志赞助的结束”，⽤约翰逊接受王室赞助的例⼦正是为了证明作者观点。 E 对。

Which of the following best describes the function of the highlighted phrase in the context of the passage as a whole? (patronage had been in decline for 50 years, yet would survive, in attenuated form, for another 50)

A It points out the most obvious implications of Johnson`s letter to his patron. 它指出了约翰逊给他的赞助人的信中最明显的含义（可能的影响（或作用、结果）；含意，暗指；牵连，涉及）。

nobility贵族；崇高，高尚

【答案】C 【题型】高亮句子功能题 【解析】该题考察高亮句作用。 选项 A，⽆法指出信的含义。信的含义在倒数第1句。 A 错。

选项 B，和动机⽆关，⾸先⽂章未写到动机，其次时间对不上。接受王室赞助是在绝交信之后很多年的事情。B错。

选项 C，⼀定要注意这⾥ qualify assertion 指的是限定、修订之前的断⾔的意思。 本句⼦开头 however 转折表示这句话⽀持作者的观点，反对经典观点。所以是修订了经典观点。C对，最准确表述了高亮句和老观点的关系。

选项 D，全⽂并未对切斯特菲尔德的忽视提供辩护。D 错。

选项 E，它驳斥的是绝交信意味着赞助时代的结束，不是赞助⼈主要从贵族中找到。 另外，王室也是贵族成员， 所以这个选项怎么都不对。 E 错。

Elizabeth Bishop`s Complete Poems(1927-1979) has come to 【seem to most of its readers】 so achieved and sufficient as a life`s work that it is hard not to lose sight of how slowly Bishop wrote poems and of how few poems, finally, she completed. But Bishop herself never ceased to find her productivity inadequate. The size and pace of her output were always in her eyes a failing (vaguely moral in complexion) for which she apologized throughout her career, although, as I will argue in this essay, Bishop`s inability to write more poems than she did was also a refusal to do so. The small, manageable size of Bishop`s body of work has facilitated its extraordinary critical reception since her death. (Robert Lowell, whose oeuvre is so much larger, has never had a complete edition of his poetry published.) Yet the size of her work is also a sign of Bishop`s alienation, that is, her uneasy, resistant relation to the literary culture that today claims her as the major poet of her generation.

伊丽莎白·毕晓普的《诗歌全集》(1927-1979)在大多数读者看来，作为一部毕生的作品，她的成就如此之高，如此之足，以至于很难不忽视毕晓普的诗歌创作速度有多慢，最后完成的诗歌有多少。但毕晓普自己却一直觉得自己的创造力不足。在她看来，她的作品的规模和速度一直是一种失败(带有模糊的道德色彩)，她在整个职业生涯中都为此道歉，尽管，正如我将在这篇文章中所论证的那样，毕晓普没有能力比她写更多的诗，也是拒绝这样做。毕晓普的作品规模小，易于管理，自她去世以来，她的作品受到了评论界的热烈欢迎。(罗伯特·洛厄尔(Robert Lowell)的作品要大得多，但他从未出版过自己的全集。)然而，她作品的规模也标志着毕晓普的异化，也就是说，她与今天声称她是她那一代主要诗人的文学文化之间的不安和抵抗关系。

Following the United States Civil War (1861-1865), many former slaves in the rural South became sharecroppers (raising a landlord`s crop for a share of the profits) or tenant farmers (selling what they raised and paying a share of the profits as rent). Most historians tend to depict these African Americans as victims of racism and the farm tenancy system. This approach, however, overlooks the role played by such African American rural reformers as Robert Lloyd Smith, founder of the Farmers' Improvement Society of Texas, and Joseph Elward Clayton, the first African American to organize farmers` institutes for the Texas Department of Agriculture, as anti-racists. Both men advocated comfortable homes and better schools for African Americans, both attributed poverty and illiteracy to causes other than racism, such as insect damage to crops, and both worked to keep Black farmers on the land, although Smith opposed farm tenancy system on Black farmers and of accommodating racism. While the extent of these reformers` influence requires more study, their organizations provided a voice for African American farmers seeking to improve their positions in the agrarian South.

sharecropper（美）收益分成的佃农

tenant

  • n.房客，租户；<法律>业主

  • v.（作为租赁者）居住，工作

racism种族主义，种族偏见；种族歧视，种族迫害

tenancy租期；租用

reformer改革家；改革运动者；改良者

anti-racist

  • adj.反种族主义的，反种族歧视的

  • n.反种族主义者

在美国内战(1861-1865)之后，南方农村的许多前奴隶变成了佃农(种植地主的作物以获得一部分利润)或佃农(出售他们种植的作物并支付一部分利润作为租金)。大多数历史学家倾向于将这些非裔美国人描述为种族主义和农场租赁制度的受害者。然而，这种方法忽视了非裔美国农村改革者所起的作用，如德克萨斯州农民改良协会的创始人罗伯特·劳埃德·史密斯和第一个为德克萨斯州农业部组织农民协会的非裔美国人约瑟夫·埃尔沃德·克莱顿，他们都是反种族主义者。两人都主张为非裔美国人提供舒适的住房和更好的学校，两人都将贫困和文盲归咎于种族主义以外的原因，如昆虫对庄稼的破坏，两人都致力于让黑人农民留在土地上，尽管史密斯反对黑人农民的农场租赁制度和纵容种族主义。虽然这些改革者的影响程度需要更多的研究，但他们的组织为寻求改善他们在南方农业地位的非裔美国农民提供了一个声音。

【文章结构分析】 文章首先描述现象：内战后，很多前奴隶成为sharecroppers或者tenant farmers。第二句介绍主流历史学家的观点：把两个黑人改革的代表人物( RLS,JEC )看作anti-racists。之后是作者的评论：两人主要是务实的改革家，尽管有反种族主义的成分。文章末句总结：尽管如何认识他们的影响有争议，他们确实作出了实际的贡献。

Throughout much of the Tertiary period( most of the past 65 million years), the Arctic supported continuous forests. Only toward the end of that period does the fossil evidence show that certain present-day Arctic plants were established and widely distributed throughout the Arctic. Many Arctic plants are thought to have originated in the high mountain ranges of central Asia and North America, to have spread northward to the Arctic as global temperatures fell in the late Tertiary, and to have achieved a circumpolar distribution by the end of the Tertiary(about 2 million years ago). However, fossil evidence to support these proposals is either lacking or fragmentary. Consequently, the routes by which these plants expanded their ranges during their colonization of the Arctic remain unknown.

the Tertiary period第三纪

Arctic

  • n.北极，北极地区

  • adj.（arctic）极度寒冷的，严寒的

  • n.（arctic）<美>御寒防水套鞋

  • v.按特定路线发送（车辆、货物或乘客）；以......线路发送（电话或其他电子信号）

在第三纪的大部分时间里(过去6500万年的大部分时间)，北极支撑着连续的森林。直到那个时期的末期，化石证据才表明，某些现今的北极植物已经建立起来，并在整个北极地区广泛分布。许多北极植物被认为起源于中亚和北美的高山山脉，在第三纪晚期全球气温下降时向北扩散到北极，并在第三纪末期(约200万年前)实现了绕极分布。然而，支持这些建议的化石证据要么缺乏，要么支离破碎。因此，这些植物在北极殖民期间扩大其活动范围的路线仍然未知。

The waters east of Cape Hangklip were once the center of a lucrative wild-caught abalone fishery, but illegal fishing in the mid-1990s escalated to such levels that the recreational fishery was closed in 2003. When abalones did not rebound, commercial fishing was also banned. Continue declines in abalone were attributed to poaching, but an invasion by rock lobsters during the early 1990s probably intensified the trend. Rock lobsters prey on sea urchins, and increased rock lobster densities coincided with significant decreases in urchins. In that area, urchins feed largely by trapping drift kelp, and in doing so provide juvenile abalone with both protective shelter and nourishment. Without urchins` presence, juvenile abalones are less likely to survive to adulthood.

汉克利普角以东的水域曾经是利润丰厚的野生鲍鱼捕捞中心，但在20世纪90年代中期，非法捕捞活动升级到如此程度，以至于休闲渔业于2003年关闭。当鲍鱼没有反弹时，商业捕捞也被禁止。鲍鱼数量的持续下降归因于偷猎，但在20世纪90年代初，岩龙虾的入侵可能加剧了这一趋势。岩龙虾以海胆为食，而岩龙虾密度的增加与海胆数量的显著减少相吻合。在那个地区，海胆主要通过捕获漂流的海带来觅食，这样做为幼鲍鱼提供了保护和营养。没有海胆的存在，幼鲍鱼很难存活到成年。

One of the reasons why many early British colonies in North America failed amid the New World`s abundance was that the settlers` mindset prevented them from living like the native inhabitants. From Native Americans, the settlers learned such skills as building brushwood weirs to trap fish, but they did not adopt the real key to success: mobility. The whole intellectual foundation of European civilization was fixity--a worldview profoundly different from that of Native Americans, who moved in response to changing food resources. Settlers were drawn to North America by tales its extraordinary abundance, not realizing that abundance is seasonal. Culture and ecological knowledge allowed Native Americans to exploit different food sources at different time of year.

mindset观念模式，思维倾向

许多早期英国在北美的殖民地在新大陆的富饶中失败的原因之一是，定居者的心态使他们无法像当地居民一样生活。移民们从印第安人那里学到了建造灌木丛堰来捕鱼等技能，但他们没有采用成功的真正关键:机动性。欧洲文明的整个智力基础是固定不变的——这是一种与美洲原住民截然不同的世界观，美洲原住民是随着食物资源的变化而迁移的。移民们被北美富饶的传说所吸引，却没有意识到富饶是季节性的。文化和生态知识使印第安人能够在一年中的不同时间开发不同的食物来源。

The author mentions "brushwood weirs" primarily in order to

A demonstrate that Native Americans provided certain forms of assistance to colonial settlers

Most popularizations of science actually do more harm than good. Why? The single most important feature of scientific work is not this or that specific result. Instead, what science accomplishes--and what physics in particular accomplishes so beautifully--is the linking of diverse phenomena, the binding together of a myriad of predictions and explanations. What nearly all popularizations do is systematically undermine the progressive reasoning that links principles, conventions, experiments, and laws. Bad science writing splinters the most interesting feature of science, its long run of connected argumentation, into isolated metaphors that last just long enough to evoke a particular result: black holes are said to be huge funnels and quantum electron orbits are characterized as diffuse clouds.

大多数科学普及实际上弊大于利。为什么?科学工作最重要的特征不是这个或那个具体的结果。相反，科学的成就——尤其是物理学的成就如此美妙——是将不同的现象联系起来，将无数的预测和解释结合在一起。几乎所有的普及所做的都是系统地破坏将原则、惯例、实验和法律联系起来的渐进推理。糟糕的科学写作将科学最有趣的特征——长期的相互关联的论证——分裂成孤立的隐喻，这些隐喻持续的时间足够长，足以引发一个特定的结果:黑洞被说成是巨大的漏斗，量子电子轨道被描述为弥漫的云。

In general, naive individuals appear more likely to learn from interaction with familiar rather than unfamiliar members of their species. Kaveliers and colleagues (2005) reported that naive laboratory-bred deer mice showed greater social learning of defensive responses to biting flies after observing responses of familiar members than after observing responses of unfamiliar members. Earlier, Valsecchi and colleagues (1996) reported striking differences in social learning of food preferences among Mongolian gerbils, depending on whether they were exposed to familiar or unfamiliar demonstrators. At the time, this was unexpected because Gaief and colleagues (1984)had previously reported no familiarity effect in Norway rats on social learning of food preferences. However, Gaief et al (1998) subsequently uncovered a significant familiarity effect that was evident when demonstrators are some hours before interacting with observers but absent when demonstrators are immediately before interacting.

While historian Linda Nicholson sees women's participation in voluntary associations as activities consistent with the increasing relegation of women`s lives to a separate, "private" sphere in nineteenth-century Europe, historian Katherine Lynch argues that these kinds of activities enabled women to join with one another（彼此结合） and to develop a kind of shadow citizenship（影子公民） within civil society, if not the formal state. These kinds of experiences were no substitute for actual political entitlements, Lynch suggests, but they deserve more attention for their importance in helping individuals forge enduring bonds of community and identity beyond domestic life. Only by limiting one`s notion of public life to formal political participation, she says, can one conclude that most women in Western society have ever been literally consigned to a separate or "private" sphere.

relegation贬谪；驱逐；移交；归属

entitlement有权得到的东西，应得的数额；权利，资格；权利感，特权感；政府津贴

forge形成，缔造；伪造，假冒；稳步前进；锻造；伪装，假冒

consign交付，运送；（为摆脱而）把……置于；把……置于(令人不快的境地)；把……交付给，把……委托给；托售；委托…代售，寄售

sphere

  • n.（活动、兴趣、专业知识的）范围，领域；球体，球，球形；社会阶层；势力范围；<文>苍穹，天，天空；<文>天体；天体外壳；地球仪

  • vt.使……成球形；包围；放入球内

【文章结构分析】 与Linda Nicholson不同，Katherine Lynch认为女性志愿者活动让女性联系到一起形成了一种非正式的公民权，形成了社会的联系，有了公共生活，而不是被限制在家庭中。

历史学家琳达·尼克尔森(Linda Nicholson)认为，在19世纪的欧洲，女性的生活越来越被置于一个独立的、“私人”的领域，女性参与志愿协会是一种与此相一致的活动，而历史学家凯瑟琳·林奇(Katherine Lynch)则认为，这些活动使女性能够相互联系，并在公民社会(如果不是正式的国家)中发展出一种影子公民身份。林奇认为，这些经历不能代替实际的政治权利，但它们在帮助个人在家庭生活之外建立持久的社区纽带和身份认同方面的重要性值得更多关注。她说，只有把一个人对公共生活的概念限制在正式的政治参与上，才能得出这样的结论:西方社会的大多数女性实际上都被委托到一个独立的或“私人”的领域。

The phrase "These kinds of experiences" in the passage refers to experiences in Lynch`s view are

A an early stage in women`s political participation

B insufficiently appreciated for their role in women`s public life

C properly assigned to the "private" sphere

D a means of altering the political structure

E historically atypical for women in Western society

【答案】B 【题型】事实信息题 【解析】题目问Lynch认为这些志愿者活动是怎么样的。文章中主线是Lynch说女性志愿者活动让女性与社会联系，不局限于私人领域。当然也有让步说志愿者活动不能替代正式的政治生活。 A.错误，Lynch认为志愿者活动是公共活动的一部分，但是并不能替代政治活动。并没有说志愿者活动是政治生活的初期阶段。 B.正确，Lynch认为志愿者活动对女性的公共生活有作用，需要更多的重视，被Nicholson之类的人低估了。 C.错误，这是和Lynch相反的观点。 D.错误，没有说过女性志愿者活动能改变政治结构。 E.错误，没有说过这种活动是不是非典型的。

The passage implies that Lynch would agree that formal political participation

A was increasingly important as the nineteenth century progressed

B was an underreported phenomenon among women in nineteenth century Europe within civil society

C is crucial to helping individuals form community ties

D is a significant component of public life

E is indicative of a kind of shadow citizenship

【答案】D 【题型】推断题 【解析】问Lynch认为正式的政治生活怎么样。文章中让步说正式的政治生活不能被志愿者活动替代；最后一句也说了公共生活并不只是政治生活，可以推出政治生活和志愿者活动都是公共生活的组成部分。

A错误，没有提到政治生活越来越重要。

B错误，没有提到女性政治生活被低估。

C错误，政治生活并不是社会联系所必须的，志愿者活动就可以帮助女性形成社会联系。

D正确，文中说了公共生活不止是政治生活，但也说了志愿者活动不能替代正式的政治生活。

E 错误，没有说政治生活和shadow citizenship之间的关系。

The male lion`s mane consists of hair of varying length and color, covering, to varying degrees, the head, neck, shoulders, and chest. Schaller suggested that the mane protects the area of the body "towards which most social contact is directed" by absorbing blows and bites. Darker mane hairs are thicker than lighter hairs, so darker manes may provide better protection. These ideas suggest that males with longer and darker manes will be wounded less frequently and/or with less severity on the area covered by the mane, but direct tests of this prediction are difficult. Individual males are seldom seen daily, and the mane itself obscures many wounds beneath it from view. Furthermore, even in the best studied population, serious fights between lions are rarely observed.

mane（马或狮子的）鬃毛；浓密的头发

blow击打

obscure

  • adj.难以说清楚的，模糊的；鲜为人知的，默默无闻的；未被查实的，不确定的；费解的，晦涩的

  • v.遮掩，遮蔽；使费解

  • n.某种模糊的或不清楚的东西

雄狮的鬃毛由不同长度和颜色的毛发组成，不同程度地覆盖在头部、颈部、肩部和胸部。夏勒认为，鬃毛通过吸收击打和咬伤来保护身体“大多数社会接触的方向”。深色的鬃毛比浅色的毛发更浓密，所以深色的鬃毛可以提供更好的保护。这些观点表明，鬃毛较长、较黑的雄性在鬃毛覆盖的区域受伤的频率和/或严重程度较低，但对这一预测的直接测试是困难的。每天很少看到雄性个体，鬃毛本身掩盖了它下面的许多伤口。此外，即使在研究得最好的种群中，也很少观察到狮子之间的激烈打斗。

【文章结构分析】 雄性狮子的鬃毛有不同的特征。S学者认为鬃毛的作用是保护雄狮的身体。且颜色更深的鬃毛要好过浅色的作用。但是目前这个结论无法验证。

Which of the following best describe the function of the highlighted portion of the passage?

A to summarize the results of an experiment

B to provide evidence on which a particular prediction is offered

C to offer a counterexample that undermines a propelled explanation

D to identify a phenomenon that Schaller found difficult to explain以确定一种夏勒认为难以解释的现象

E to explain the variation among individual manes

【答案】B 【题型】高亮句子功能题 【解析】题目考察句子在整个文章中起到的作用。句子作题的解题关键在于对句间关系的把握，高亮句后句开头“these idea suggests that”，表示高亮句本身引发了一个推论，一个很难被验证的预测 “but direct tests of this prediction are difficult”。根据对句间关系的考察，B选项最符合。

A选项experiment在文中找不到依据

C选项高亮句与前后句都是同向关系，没有转折提示词，所以不存在“undermine”

D选项difficult to explain的不是高亮句而是下一句

E选项解释个体之间的变化与高亮句无关，且文中未提及

A divide between aesthetic and technical considerations has played a crucial role in mapmaking and cartographic scholarship. Since nineteenth century cartographers, for instance, understood themselves as technicians who did not care about visual effects, while others saw themselves as landscape painters. That dichotomy structured the discipline of the history of cartography. Until the 1980s, in what Blakemore and Harley called "the 'Old is Beautiful' paradigm," scholars largely focused on maps made before 1800, marveling at their beauty and sometimes regretting the decline of the pre-technical age. Early mapmaking was considered art while modern cartography was located within the realm of engineering utility. Alpers, however, has argued that this boundary would have puzzled mapmakers in the seventeenth century, because they considered themselves to be visual engineers.

cartographic地图的；制图的

  • n.遗憾，惋惜；（因无法出席会议、聚会等的）致歉语

  • n.（煤气、水、电等的）公共服务，公用事业；（供电、供水等的）公用事业单位；应用程序，实用程序；实用，有用；<澳>小卡车，轻型货车；（博弈论，经济学）效用

  • adj.有用的，多功能的

美学和技术考虑之间的分歧在地图制作和制图学术中发挥了至关重要的作用。例如，自19世纪以来，制图师认为自己是不关心视觉效果的技术人员，而其他人则认为自己是风景画家。这种二分法构建了地图学历史这门学科。直到20世纪80年代，在布莱克莫尔和哈雷所称的“老即是美”范式中，学者们主要关注1800年以前绘制的地图，惊叹于它们的美丽，有时也为前技术时代的衰落感到遗憾。早期的地图制作被认为是一门艺术，而现代地图学则属于工程实用领域。然而，阿尔珀斯认为，这个界限会让17世纪的地图绘制者感到困惑，因为他们认为自己是视觉工程师。

【文章结构分析】 本文时间线索较复杂。

首句总体陈述：审美和技术考虑的对立是地图绘图界的重要矛盾。

从19世纪（1800后），绘图者多数把自己当作技师，不强调视觉效果，而另一些把自己当作地形画家。直到1980年，正如B&H称谓的“旧的是美的典范”，学者们关注1800年之前的地图，惊奇于其艺术美，哀叹前技术时代艺术性的衰落。早期地图制作被当作艺术，而现代绘图属于实用工程技能领域。末句，作者引用Alpers观点：艺术与技术的边界区分会让17世纪（1600年-1700年）的地图制作者困惑，因为他们把自己当作“视觉工程师”（强调艺术和技巧的统一）。

Many cultural anthropologists have come to reject the scientific framework of empiricism that dominated the field until the 1970s and now regard all scientific knowledge as socially constructed. They argue that information about cultures during the empiricist era typically came from anthropologists who brought with them a prepackaged set of conscious and unconscious biases. Cultural anthropology, according to the post-1970s critique, is unavoidably subjective, and the anthropologist should be explicit in acknowledging that fact. Anthropology should stop striving to build a better database about cultural behavior and should turn to developing a more humanistic interpretation of cultures. The new framework holds that it may be more enlightening to investigate the biases of earlier texts than to continue with empirical methodologies.

post-1970s 1970后的

investigate侦察（某事）；调查（某人）；研究

investment投资；值得买的东西；（时间、精力的）投入；<旧>包围，封锁

许多文化人类学家已经开始拒绝在20世纪70年代之前主导该领域的经验主义的科学框架，现在他们认为所有的科学知识都是社会建构的。他们认为，在经验主义时代，关于文化的信息通常来自人类学家，他们带来了一套预先包装好的有意识和无意识的偏见。根据20世纪70年代后的批评，文化人类学不可避免地是主观的，人类学家应该明确承认这一事实。人类学应该停止努力建立一个更好的关于文化行为的数据库，而应该转向发展一种更人性化的文化解释。新的框架认为，调查早期文本的偏见可能比继续使用经验方法更有启发性。

Writing about nineteenth-century women`s travel writing, Lila Harper notes that the four women she discussed used their own names, in contrast with the nineteenth-century female novelists who either published anonymously or used male pseudonyms. The novelists doubtless realized that they were breaking boundaries, whereas three of the four daring, solitary travelers espoused traditional values, eschewing radicalism and women`s movements. Whereas the female novelists criticized their society, the female travelers seemed content to leave society as it was while accomplishing their own liberation. In other words, they lived a contradiction. For the subjects of Harper`s study, solitude in both the private and public spheres prevailed-a solitude that conferred authority, hitherto a male prerogative, but that also precluded any collective action or female solidarity.

莱拉·哈珀(Lila Harper)在谈到19世纪女性旅行写作时指出，她所讨论的四位女性都使用了自己的名字，而19世纪的女性小说家要么匿名发表作品，要么使用男性笔名。毫无疑问，小说家们意识到他们正在打破界限，而四位勇敢、孤独的旅行者中有三位信奉传统价值观，避开激进主义和妇女运动。女性小说家对社会进行了批判，而女性旅行者似乎满足于在实现自我解放的同时离开社会。换句话说，他们生活在矛盾之中。对于哈珀的研究对象来说，无论是在私人领域还是在公共领域，孤独都是普遍存在的——这种孤独赋予了权威，迄今为止，这是男性的特权，但也排除了任何集体行动或女性团结。

Although vastly popular during its time, much nineteenth-century women`s fiction in the United States went unread by the twentieth-century educated elite, who were taught to ignore it as didactic. However, American literature has a tradition of didacticism going back to its Puritan roots, shifting over time from sermons and poetic transcripts into novels, which proved to be perfect vehicles for conveying social values. In the nineteenth century, critics reviled Poe for neglecting to conclude his stories with pithy moral tags, while Longfellow was canonized for his didactic verse. Although rhetorical changes favoring the anti-didactic can be detected as nineteenth-century American transformed itself into a secular society, it was twentieth-century criticism, which placed aesthetic value above everything else, that had no place in its doctrine for the didacticism of others.

尽管19世纪的女性小说在当时非常受欢迎，但20世纪受过教育的精英们却没有读过很多女性小说，因为他们被教导要把它当作说教而忽略。然而，美国文学有一种说教的传统，可以追溯到它的清教徒根源，随着时间的推移，从布道和诗歌手稿转变为小说，小说被证明是传达社会价值观的完美工具。在19世纪，评论家们痛斥爱伦·坡没有在小说结尾加上简洁的道德标签，而朗费罗则因其说教式的诗句而受到推崇。尽管在十九世纪的美国向世俗社会转变的过程中，可以发现倾向于反说教的修辞变化，但将美学价值置于一切之上的二十世纪的批评，在其教义中没有为他人的说教主义留下一席之地。

【文章结构分析】 文章首句给出现象及可能的原因解释：19世纪女性小说当时很流行，但被20世纪的精英读者冷落，说教是可能的原因。二句however转折，作者提出对首句解释观点的反驳：美国文学有说教传统。在19世纪，忽视道德说教的小说被批评，有说教的被赞扬。作者最后给出自己认为正确的原因解释：是二十世纪的美国变成了世俗社会，是二十世纪的评论者，把审美标准放置在所有其他标准上面。

During the Pleistocene epoch, several species of elephants isolated on islands underwent rapid dwarfing. This phenomenon was not necessarily confined to the Pleistocene, but may have occurred much earlier in the Southeastern Asian islands, although evidence is fragmentary. Several explanations are possible for this dwarfing. For example, islands often have not been colonized by large predators or are too small to hold viable predator populations. Once free from predation pressure, large body size is of little advantage to herbivores. Additionally, island habitats have limited food resources, a smaller body size and a need for fewer resources would thus be favored. Interestingly, the island rule is reversed for small mammals such as rodents, for which gigantism is favored under insular conditions.

dwarf

  • n.（神话中有魔法的）小矮人；侏儒，矮子；矮星

  • v.使显得矮小，使相形见绌

  • adj.矮小的，矮种的

  • v.限制，局限；防止……扩散；关押，监禁；使离不开（或受困于床、轮椅等）

  • n.边界，范围；限制，局限

viable可望成功的，切实可行的；能存活的，能生长发育的

在更新世时期，一些被隔离在岛屿上的大象物种经历了迅速的侏儒化。这种现象并不一定局限于更新世，而可能在更早的时候就发生在东南亚岛屿上，尽管证据是零碎的。这种矮化现象有几种可能的解释。例如，岛屿通常没有被大型食肉动物殖民，或者太小而无法容纳可生存的食肉动物种群。一旦摆脱了捕食的压力，大体型对食草动物来说就没有什么优势了。此外，岛屿栖息地的食物资源有限，体型较小，对资源的需求较少，因此会受到青睐。有趣的是，对于啮齿类动物等小型哺乳动物来说，岛屿规则是相反的，它们在岛屿条件下更倾向于巨人症。

In the early twentieth century, small magazines and the innovative graphics used on them created the face of the avant-guard. It was a look that signaled progressive ideas and unconventionality because it dispensed with the cardinal rule of graphic design: to take an idea and make it visually clear, concise, and instantly understood. Instead, graphics produced by avant-guard artists exclusively for the avant-guard (as opposed to their advertising work) were usually difficult to decipher, ambiguous, or nonsensical. This overturning of convention, this assailing of standard graphic and typographic formats, was part of a search for intellectual freedom. The impulse toward liberation enabled avant-guardists to see with fresh eyes untried possibilities for arranging and relating words and images on paper.

progressive进步的，先进的；逐步发生的，逐步发展的；向前移动的

unconventionality非常规；异常

conventionality惯例；习俗；老套

dispense发放，分配；提供，施予；配（药），发（药）

(metaphor隐喻，暗喻；象征，标志)

typographic排字上的；印刷上的

intellectual freedom智识自由：允许人们思考或研究他们想要的内容的自由。

在二十世纪早期，小型杂志及其上使用的创新图形创造了先锋派的面貌。这是一种标志着进步思想和非传统的外观，因为它摒弃了平面设计的基本规则:采取一个想法，使其在视觉上清晰、简洁，并立即被理解。相反，由前卫艺术家专门为前卫制作的图形(与他们的广告作品相反)通常难以破译，模棱两可或荒谬。这种对传统的颠覆，对标准图形和排版格式的攻击，是对知识自由的追求的一部分。解放的冲动使先锋派以全新的眼光看到了在纸上安排和联系文字和图像的未经尝试的可能性。

According to the passage, the primary purpose of conventional graphic design is to

A render unpopular ideas palatable to a wider audience

B capture readers` attention with bold fonts

C communicate nonsensical notions to a wide public

D communicate ideas as efficiently and unambiguously as possible

E introduce previously unknown ideas to the general public

render渲染

palatable美味的，可口的；愉快的

bold fonts粗体字

答案：D

According to the passage, avant-guard artists of the early twentieth-century created ambiguous or nonsensical graphics as part of an attempt to

A expand the potential for expression through visual art

B compete with advertisements for reader`s attention

C encourage the expansion of small magazines

答案：A

From 1910 to 1913, women suffragists in the United States organized annual parades--activity traditionally conducted by men to proclaim solidarity in some cause--not only as a public expression of suffragist solidarity but also a conscious transgression of the rules of social order: women's very presence in the streets challenged traditional notions of femininity and restrictions on women's conduct. While recognizing the parade's rhetorical force as a vehicle for social change, scholars have recently begun to examine its drawbacks as a form of protest. Lumsden characterizes the American suffrage parade as a "double-edged sword", arguing that women's efforts to proclaim their solidarity left them open to patronizing commentary from press and public and to organized opposition from antisuffragists.

suffragist妇女政权论者；参政权扩大论者

solidarity团结一致

transgression [地质] 海侵；犯罪；违反；逸出

presence出席，存在；<正式>（某人的）所在地方

rhetorical（与）修辞（有关）的；反问的，反诘的；巧辩的，说话虚夸的

vehicle交通工具，车辆；（实现目的的）工具，媒介

suffrage选举权；投票；参政权；代祷；赞成票

patronizing

  • v.以高人一等的态度对待；（经常）惠顾；赞助（patronize 的现在分词）

  • adj.（说话、行为）自认为高人一等的

从1910年到1913年，美国的妇女参政权论者组织了一年一度的游行——传统上由男性进行的活动，以宣布对某些事业的团结——不仅是妇女参政权论者团结的公开表达，也是对社会秩序规则的有意识的违反:妇女在街上的出现挑战了传统的女性观念和对妇女行为的限制。虽然承认游行的修辞力量是社会变革的工具，但学者们最近开始研究它作为一种抗议形式的缺点。拉姆斯登将美国争取选举权的游行描述为一把“双刃剑”，她认为妇女们宣称团结一致的努力使她们容易受到媒体和公众傲慢的评论，也容易受到反妇女参政主义者有组织的反对。

【文章结构分析】 文章首先描述现象：1910年至1913年，美国女性选举权主义者组织了游行。传统上，游行是男性表达团结、破坏秩序规则的活动。女性游行挑战了传统对女性的概念，对女性行为的限制。While句介绍最近学者们对女性游行负面作用的理解：女性要求团结的努力导致媒体和公众的怜悯同情，也招致反女权主义者的反对。

Unlike most Jane Austen scholarship before 1980, much recent scholarship analyzes the novels of Austen, who lived from 1775 to 1817, in the context of Austen's tumultuous times, which saw the French and American revolutions and the Napoleonic Wars. Yet Frantz notes another revolution, rarely mentioned in Austen scholarship: the Great Masculine Renunciation that altered conventions in men's dress and behavior. During the later eighteenth century, wealthy gentlemen exchanged the velvets and satins long in fashion for somber woolen suits. Frantz contends that this change reflected deeper cultural changes. The value(价值观) once placed on men's expressiveness, reflected in Mackenzie's novel The Man of Feeling (1771), gave way to a preference for emotional restraint. In Austen's novels, the heroine often struggles to glimpse the true nature of hero beneath his reserved exterior.

Jane Austen简·奥斯汀：英国小说家，以描写中产阶级家庭生活为主，作品包括《傲慢与偏见》、《理智与情感》等。

tumultuous吵闹的；骚乱的；狂暴的

the Napoleonic Wars拿破仑战争

与1980年之前的大多数简·奥斯丁研究不同，最近的许多研究都是在奥斯丁生活的动荡时代的背景下分析她的小说的。奥斯丁生于1775年至1817年，经历了法国和美国的革命以及拿破仑战争。然而，弗朗茨注意到另一场革命，在奥斯汀的研究中很少提及:“伟大的男性放弃”改变了男性的着装和行为习惯。在18世纪后期，富有的绅士们把流行已久的天鹅绒和缎子换成了阴沉的羊毛套装。Frantz认为，这种变化反映了更深层次的文化变化。麦肯齐的小说《有感情的人》(1771)反映出，曾经重视男人的表现力的价值观，现在让位于对情感克制的偏好。在奥斯丁的小说中，女主人公常常努力去窥见男主角含蓄的外表下的真实本性。

Whereas Carlos Bulosan aimed through fiction and personal testimony to advance both Filipino civil rights in the United States and the social transformation of the Philippines, Yen Le Espiritu has set herself the task of recovering life histories of Filipino Americans. Her work brings Filipino Americans of the generation following the 1934-1965 immigration hiatus graphically to life. A special strength is the representation of Filipino American women, who were scarce among immigrants before the 1934 American curb on Filipino immigration but composed more than half of the immigrants to America since liberalization in 1965. Espiritu`s subjects document their changing sense of Filipino identity in the United States, much as Bulosan did as a member of the first substantial wave of immigrants.

Carlos Bulosan的目标是通过小说和个人证词来推进菲律宾人在美国的公民权利和菲律宾的社会转型，而Yen Le Espiritu则为自己设定了恢复菲律宾裔美国人生活史的任务。她的作品生动地描绘了1934-1965年移民中断后的一代菲律宾裔美国人。在1934年美国限制菲律宾移民之前，菲律宾裔美国妇女在移民中很少，但在1965年自由化以来，她们占美国移民的一半以上，这是一个特殊的优势。埃斯皮里图的拍摄对象记录了他们在美国的菲律宾身份认同感的变化，就像布洛桑作为第一波大规模移民中的一员一样。
