Passage 225 Easy

Ecologists study how millions of species share the world, rather than take on the whole planet at once, they generally focus on a single ecosystem, be it a prairie, a tidal flat, or a sand dune. Even within those limits, they are frustrated by porous frontiers. As a result, ecologists have done some of their most important work on islands, nature`s own isolated laboratories, which may be colonized only a few times over the course of millions of years. On them, ecologists have figured out how the size of a given habitat determine how many species it can support. They have then applied that knowledge to the mainland, showing how fragmented ecosystems become like archipelagoes, where extinctions can strike.

 

prairie （北美的）大草原；蒸气火车头（Prairie）

tidal 潮汐的，受潮汐影响的

flat

  • adj.平的，水平的；平坦的；（水面）平静的，波澜不兴的；平滑的；平放的，平躺的，平卧的；足弓平坦的；扁平的；（鞋）平跟的，低跟的；断然的，直截了当的；（费率、价格等）统一的，固定的；（市场、价格等）疲软的，萧条的；枯燥的，无趣的，缺乏热情的；（饮品）走了气的；（轮胎）没气的，瘪的；（电池）电力不足的，没电的；平淡的，无变化的；（音符）降半音的；音调偏低的；色彩单调的，无反差的，无景深的；无光泽的；（图表上的线）平的，无变化的；（组织或系统）内部层次不多的；（关于）无障碍平地赛马的；（面包）未发酵的

  • adv.水平地；平整地；平贴着；正好；完全地，彻底地；音调偏低地

  • n.<英>公寓，单元房；（通常指近水的）浅滩，洼地；（某物的）平面部份；（音符的）降半音；降半音符号；<美>浅箱，浅苗床；平底鞋，低跟鞋（flats）；漏气轮胎；平板列车，敞车，平台货车；平面布景，布景屏；无障碍平地赛马季节（the Flat）

dune （由风吹积而成的）沙丘

porous 多孔渗水的；能渗透的；有气孔的

archipelago 群岛，列岛；多岛的海区

 

生态学家研究数以百万计的物种如何共享这个世界，而不是同时研究整个地球，他们通常只关注一个生态系统，无论是草原、滩涂还是沙丘。即使在这些范围内，他们也会因边界漏洞百出而感到沮丧。因此，生态学家在岛屿上完成了一些最重要的工作，这些岛屿是大自然自己孤立的实验室，在数百万年的时间里可能只被殖民过几次。在这些岛屿上，生态学家们弄清了特定栖息地的大小如何决定它能养活多少物种。然后，他们把这些知识应用到大陆上，展示了支离破碎的生态系统是如何变得像群岛一样，在那里可能会发生物种灭绝。

 

It can be inferred that the term "porous frontiers" is used to refer to

A a tendency for the area of an ecosystem to shrink

B human-caused processes that alter the character of an ecosystem

C movement of species into an ecosystem from outside

D variation in what the term "ecosystem" signifies

E lack of protection for endangered habitats

 

【答案】C

porous: easy to pass or get through

关键词 porous frontiers 前面说了 focus on a single ecosystem， 后面说了在 nature`s own isolated laboratories 中做实验，都表示 porous frontiers 应该是不独立造成的问题，也就是对应C选项说的问题。

 

In the context in which it appears, "isolated" most nearly means

A completely uncontaminated 

B somewhat unusual 

C extremely rare

D relatively inaccessible

E strictly confined

正确答案： D

 

Passage 226 Easy

The border decoration in medieval manuscripts referred to as pen flourishing reached great artistic heights in the northern Netherlands in the 1400s. The regional variants in form that evolved make flourishing a useful tool for localizing and roughly dating manuscripts. When the first printed books appeared in that region, many copies were still traditionally decorated by hand with such flourishing. Since books` publication can usually be dated with far more accuracy than manuscripts, studying these decorations in early printed books might lead to a more precise dating of the penwork in manuscripts. It is of less help in localizing the flourishing. Upon completion, copies of printed books were often sold unadorned, to be decorated elsewhere as commissioned by their buyers.

 

flourishing

  • adj.繁荣，蓬勃发展

  • v.繁荣，昌盛；挥动；（植物或动物）长势好，茁壮成长（flourish 的现在分词）

commission

  • n.考察团，委员会；佣金，回扣；犯罪；委托，命令；（军队中的）官职，军衔；（尤指艺术品）委托制作；<古>所授之权，代办权

  • v.委托撰写，委托制作；委任，任命……为军官；（使军舰）正式使用，服现役

 

中世纪手稿中的边框装饰被称为 “繁笔”，在 14 世纪的荷兰北部达到了极高的艺术水平。这种形式的地区变异使繁饰成为一种有用的工具，可用于确定手稿的位置和大致年代。当第一批印刷书籍在该地区出现时，许多副本仍沿用传统的手工装饰方式。由于书籍的出版年代通常比手稿要准确得多，研究早期印刷书籍中的这些装饰可能有助于更精确地确定手稿中的笔迹年代。但这对确定繁饰的位置帮助不大。印刷书籍完成后，通常不加任何装饰就出售，然后根据购买者的要求在其他地方进行装饰。

 

Which of the following best describes the function of the highlighted sentence?

A It points out a difficulty involved in studying pen flourishing 它指出了研究笔的兴盛所涉及的一个困难

B It restates an assertion about the first printed books 它重申了关于第一批印刷书籍的论断

C It corrects a misconception regarding the decoration of manuscripts 它纠正了关于手稿装饰的一个误解

D It provides support for a claim about the dating of printed books 支持了关于印刷书籍年代的说法

E It summarized an argument about how to interpret certain type of penwork. 它总结了关于如何解释某些类型的钢笔作品的论点。

正确答案： A

高亮句是对前面句子 It is of less help in localizing the flourishing. 的一个总结，这个总结就是 a difficulty involved in studying pen flourishing

 

According to the passage, pen flourishing in manuscripts can provide historians with valuable information about 

A who commissioned the manuscript

B the source from which the manuscript was copied

C the value placed on the contents of the manuscript

D where the manuscript was produced

E the collaborative process used to produce the manuscript

答案：D

A 没说是谁

B 没说 source 是什么

C 没提到手稿内容的价值

D pen flourishing 确实可以用来确定手稿是哪里生产的

E 没提到撰写稿件的合作过程

 

这题特别误导人的地方在于，他虽然前边几句就交待了手稿是既可以dating也可以localizing的，但是后来话题一转大部分内容都在说书本的事，然后又说书本不能localize。实际上只要明确手稿和书本是不同的东西，这题就好理解（可能这对外国人来说是一目了然的，但是non-native就很晕）。

 

Passage 228 Medium

A recent exhibition of works by late-nineteenth-century painters Mary Cassatt, Berthe Morisot, and Eva Gonzales offered a rich visual counterpart to studies focusing new attention on the social and ideological forces that influenced their work. The paintings by Gonzales were particularly illuminating. Long marginalized by scholars as little more than an apprentice of Edouard Manet, Gonzales is revealed by the exhibition as possessing remarkable, if uneven, talents. Given the exhibition`s focus, and especially the provocative new emphasis on Gonzales, the accompanying catalog proved disappointing. There often-quoted essays by critics contemporary to the artists- essays in themselves noteworthy but historical artifacts nonetheless-provided the exhibition with its only critical readings. Thus, a significant opportunity for scholarly debate was not only lost but even seemed pointedly avoided.

 

illuminating

  • adj.照亮的，照明的；启蒙的，有启发性的

  • v.照明，阐释（illuminate 的现在分词形式）

apprentice

  • n.学徒，徒弟；生手，新手

  • v.收……为学徒；当学徒

provocative

  • adj.挑衅的，煽动性的；挑逗的，激发性欲的；引发思考的，启发性的

  • n.刺激物，挑拨物

marginalize 排斥；忽视；使处于社会边缘；使脱离社会发展进程

 

最近举办的十九世纪晚期画家玛丽-卡萨特、贝尔特-莫里索和伊娃-冈萨雷斯的作品展为研究提供了丰富的视觉对应，这些研究对影响他们作品的社会和意识形态力量给予了新的关注。冈萨雷斯的绘画作品尤其具有启发性。长期以来，冈萨雷斯一直被学者们边缘化，认为他不过是爱德华-马奈的一个学徒而已，但展览却揭示了冈萨雷斯的非凡才能，尽管这种才能参差不齐。鉴于展览的重点，尤其是对冈萨雷斯的新强调，随展目录令人失望。目录中经常引用与艺术家同时代的评论家的文章--这些文章本身值得一提，但毕竟是历史文物--为展览提供了唯一的批评性解读。因此，学术讨论的重要机会不仅失去了，甚至似乎被刻意回避了。

 

最后两句话也是看了好久才大概知道什么意思。考虑到展览的重点，特别是对Gonzales的革新性的强调，随附的目录却让人失望了。这些经常被引用的、和艺术家同时代的评论家的论文，（尽管这些论文本身是显著的，但仍然是历史作品）提供了这次展览唯一的评论性的内容。因此，一个重要的学术性辩论的机会不仅是被错过了，而且似乎是故意被避免了。随附的目录指的就是这些论文，因为这些论文的作者和Gonzales是同时代的，所以他们对Gonzales的评价是偏向于贬义的（参考前文Long marginalized by scholars as little more than an apprentice of Edouard Manet），鉴于作者认为Gonzales的作品是令人发醒的，所以这里说随附的目录让人失望了。

 

Select the sentence in which the author describes and counters an assessment of a particular artist.

 

请选出作者对某位艺术家的评价进行描述和反驳的句子。

 

正确答案： Long marginalized by scholars as little more than an apprentice of Edouard Manet, Gonzales is revealed by the exhibition as possessing remarkable, if uneven, talents

 

In the context in which it appears, "counterpart to" most nearly means

A duplicate of 

B alternate to

C complement to

D opposite of

E emblem of

 

counterpart 对应的人（或事物）；（法律文件的）副本

duplicate

  • v.复制，复印；（无必要地）重复（某事）；使成倍增加

  • adj.完全一样的，复制的；二重的

  • n.完全一样的东西，复制品

alternate

  • adj.轮流的，交替的；间隔的；供选择的，备用的；（叶，芽）互生的；另类的

  • v.（使）交替，（使）轮流

  • n.替补者，候补者

complement

  • v.补充，补足

  • n.补足物，衬托物；足数，足额；补语；余角

 

Passage 238 Easy

Scholars have tended to treat the ideas of American social reformer Jane Addams as unique, failing to compare them sufficiently those of other social activists and public intellectuals. Recent work, however, has situated her more thoroughly in the thinking and events of her time. For example, labor historians have usefully contextualized Addams` close work with labor unions in the 1890s. When Addams` interest in the workers` reform agenda is understood in relation to the history of trade unionism in Chicago and its impressive record of political action, her contribution emerges as far more cooperative than groundbreaking. Workers influenced her in ways not preciously appreciated. Such contextualizing efforts make it possible to see what Addams learned from other reformers and what she contributed herself.

 

contextualize 置于上下文（或背景）中

unionism 工会主义；联合主义；联邦主义

 

学者们往往将美国社会改革家简-亚当斯的思想视为独一无二的，而没有将其与其他社会活动家和公共知识分子的思想进行充分比较。然而，最近的研究将她更全面地纳入了她所处时代的思想和事件中。例如，劳工史学家对 1890 年代亚当斯与工会的密切合作进行了有益的背景分析。如果将亚当斯对工人改革议程的兴趣与芝加哥工会史及其令人印象深刻的政治行动记录联系起来理解，她的贡献就会发现合作性远远大于开创性。工人对她的影响并未得到珍视。通过这种背景分析，我们可以看到亚当斯从其他改革者那里学到了什么，她自己又做出了什么贡献。

 

The primary purpose of the passage is to

A criticize Addams for not realizing the extent of her debt to other social activists and public intellectuals

B describe how scholars have misunderstood Addams` ideas regarding social reform

C outline a debate within the historical community regarding Addams` approach to social reform

D emphasize the importance of placing Addams` work in a larger framework of reform and activism

E discuss the impact of Addams` close work with labor union on working conditions in the 1890s

 

正确答案： D

A：没提到 criticize

B：可以从关键字how入手，文章其实没有提到how

C：没提到 debate

E：没提到 impact

 

The author refers to the "history of trade unionism in Chicago"primarily as

A an issue that has been largely ignored by historians

B an issue that has inspired contention among historians

C a model for how trade unionists might engage in political action

D an area in which Addams` contributions have been underestimated

E a valuable context for understanding the nature of Addams` contributions

 

答案：E

A 历史学家大多忽视了这一问题

B 引发历史学家争论的问题

C 是工会成员如何参与政治行动的典范

D Addams 的贡献被低估的一个领域

E 是理解 Addams 贡献性质的重要背景
